Japan's Foreign Trade Surplus 111

Japanese United News, Tokyo, 30th – Japan's foreign trade, which had a monthly trade deficit since the beginning of the year, turned to a surplus in the sixth month. Trade in late June created a surplus of 10 million yuan. The main reason is that cotton imports have entered a slack period, and the import of other important import goods such as wool fertilizer soybean cake has come to an end. The import of wood and groceries is gradually decreasing. On the export side, raw silk is still at the amount of 14,000 bales, and cotton textiles have reached a record figure of 9.66 million yuan due to the fall of the Japanese exchange rate.

From Today, the Japanese Government Manages Exchange Rates to Prevent Capital Outflow 112

Reuters, Tokyo, 30th – Two important financial bills passed by the recent special session of parliament will take effect on July 1. One is a plan to prevent capital outflow, which will result in the government managing exchange rates, and the other is a currency conversion law, which will increase the maximum limit of banknotes issued by the Bank of Japan to 1,000,000,000 yuan, compared to the current limit of 120,000,000 yuan.

Important News

Tokyo *Manchōhō* Discusses the Second World War 113

Advocating Taking the Offensive Against the United States First

Seizing Maritime Power in the Pacific

Occupying the Philippines and Hawaii

As Easy as Reaching into a Pocket

The *Tokyo Manchōhō* recently published an article discussing the Second World War. The translation is as follows, in order to show the Japanese perspective: (1) The Focus of World Diplomacy Shifts to the Pacific – The confrontation of European countries centered on the Mediterranean Sea, and the rivalry between Britain and the United States across the Atlantic Ocean, have become past facts of diplomacy. Today, the opposition between Japan, the United States, and Russia, centered on the Chinese mainland, and the intensification of political and economic issues, are even greater than in the past. In essence, the so-called Pacific situation has become the focus of world diplomacy. In this major situation, Japan's foreign policy should be based on all the phenomena on the Chinese mainland, and there is no doubt that it should establish and implement a direction. What, after all, is the essence of the opposition between Japan, the United States, and Russia, centered on the Chinese mainland? The world often says that the crisis between Japan and the United States started with the Manchurian Incident last autumn, but in fact, the hidden danger between Japan and the United States was in a precarious situation several times after the Russo-Japanese War. For example, the Korean independence movement and the anti-Japanese issue in Southern California, etc., have long made Japan's feelings towards the United States icy and coal-like. Until the Russo-Japanese War, the United States openly abandoned the Atlantic Ocean and shifted its gaze to the Chinese mainland in the Pacific Ocean. At that time, the United States used the open door and equal opportunity in Manchuria as slogans for the Russo-Japanese War. John Hay's strong effort to steer world opinion towards the Manchurian proposition was especially the most obvious point of its intention. However, although the United States schemed in this way, in fact, Manchuria has passed through 25 long years, until today, whether it is industry, commerce, or investment, the fact that its position has been monopolized by Japan is also due to geographical relations. The biggest point is that the political and military power of the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway has become firmly established. Remembering the attempts by the United States after the Treaty of Portsmouth to buy the South Manchuria Railway, infringe on the South Manchuria Railway's monopoly, lay the Jinai Railway, and advocate the neutrality of the South Manchuria Railway, etc., all focus on the Manchurian and Mongolian problems. Unfortunately, Japan's power has already been established, and the United States was still feeling uneasy about the environment in the Atlantic at that time, so it was unable to concentrate on expanding its power in the Pacific. Since the outbreak of the European War, the United States has taken the opportunity to develop towards the Chinese mainland. It once declared: "The policy of the United States is to solve the permanent security and peace of China, to strive to maintain the security of China's territory and administration, and to guarantee all the rights of friendly countries in accordance with treaties and international law, so as to establish an impartial principle of commerce throughout China." This declaration was the beginning of the United States' support for its power in the Asian continent. By the time of the World War, the United States' trade with China gradually expanded, but at the same time, Japan had monopolized the East Asian market, so it was quite jealous of the United States. At this time, the conflict of interests between Japan and the United States has become unavoidable. Unexpectedly, the Manchurian Incident broke out, and the imperial army occupied all the main areas of Manchuria. The United States, harboring private grievances, then proposed the Non-War Treaty to prevent the action of our army. At the time of the Jinzhou attack, the United States again used the Nine-Power Treaty to stir up the world's attention and restrict the action of our army. After the establishment of the new state of Manchuria, the United States instigated the League of Nations to hinder the development of the state of Manchuria. All kinds of attitudes have made our people resentful. Although, the empire's claim to Manchuria will never change due to its obstruction. No third country can interfere with the empire's actions. Nevertheless, the Manchurian problem cannot yet be considered safe. On one hand, we must wait for the interim report of the League of Nations to decide what to do. At the same time, we must also see what the future policy of the United States towards China will be. If it is more persistent in its preconceived notions, and wants to drive out Japan's power on the Chinese mainland, that is, to seek to succeed Britain's power in the Chinese market, so as to suppress the expansion of Japan's power, then a head-on conflict between Japan and the United States is feared to be not far away. (2) The Second World War: After the end of the European War, human society around the world, in view of the cruelty of the war, is singing the praises of peace, hoping to avoid the recurrence of tragic acts. However, when we examine in detail the past history of human struggle, if we want to seek the survival of mankind, we cannot eliminate future struggles. The recent Manchurian and Shanghai incidents are still small movements of struggle. When we deduce the causes and results of the two major incidents, we are afraid that the Second World War will be difficult to avoid. The various great powers behind a certain country are enough to destroy world peace. Moreover, in recent years, the eyes of various countries have been concentrated on the Far East, and the Liaodong Peninsula in the Far East is nothing more than the Balkans of the East. As far as northern Manchuria is concerned, it is an indispensable resource area for our survival, which coincides with a certain region centered on defending France during the European War. Therefore, we predict that in the Second World War, Japan and the United States will have a fierce struggle in the Pacific, but it is only a matter of time. Look at Britain today, building a large naval base in Singapore, and rushing to equip modern warships. Why is that? Britain's hegemony over the world with its navy is its traditional policy. It is now also in view of the changing situation in the Pacific, fearing that the equipment in Australia and New Zealand is not complete, so it has to step up its defense. The Soviet Union, which is eyeing the opportunity in the north, is also quietly watching the opportunity to advance and retreat in the Far East. Therefore, an ominous situation has suddenly appeared in the Pacific, and various crises are gradually lurking. In addition, the United States, before 1898 in the 31st year of Meiji, annexed the Hawaiian Islands and built a naval base in the Pacific. The following year, it acquired the Philippines, and the threat to Japan increased day by day. The Asian control policy that the United States holds must first conquer Japan, and Japan is suffering from overpopulation, and it has to develop outward. If the United States wants to suppress Japan's outward development, then Japan, for the sake of self-defense, cannot sit still and wait for death. It must decide the outcome with the United States. Recently, since the United States implemented anti-Japanese measures, the inevitability of the Japanese-American War has been recognized by those in the know. Recently, the concentration of the entire US fleet in the Pacific, its provocative actions, is enough to arouse the long-standing resentment of our people against the United States, and the situation is quite dangerous. When we look at the strength of the US fleet as a whole, it is weaker than our Japanese Combined Fleet. If it encounters an emergency, Japan, if it launches an offensive first, can seize the maritime power of the Pacific, occupy the Philippines and Hawaii, as easily as reaching into a pocket. At that time, if Japan attacked the Panama Canal and drove straight in, it would deeply regret interfering in the affairs of the East. In short, our Japan will not allow other countries to interfere in the Chinese problem. If peaceful methods are not easy to solve, then there is only one way to fight with force.

Recent Situation of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers in Northeastern China over the Past Week 114

The Gong and Feng Armies Urgently Rush Towards Yushu

Ma Zhanshan's Army Shifts to the Hulai Route

Li Du's Troops Counterattack Towards Yilan

Harbin Correspondence: Lately, the battles in Jilin and Heilongjiang have become increasingly fierce. Within Jilin Province, the Self-Defense Army led by Gong and Feng, among others, has largely shifted towards Yushu and Fuyu, heading towards Changchun. The troops of Li and Ding have gathered in Boli and exited through Sanxing, while the National Salvation Army led by Wang Delin has seized Dunhua, and Jiang Haishan's troops have advanced towards Hunchun, attacking Jiandao. The Broadsword Brigade of Xing Zhanqing is scattered between Yimianpo, Ashe River, and Shuangcheng, Acheng, to contain the Japanese army, allowing the Self-Defense Army and National Salvation Army to operate. In recent times, the battles at Dongguansuo in Shuangcheng and the battles along the Qike Line (Qiqihar to Keshan via Nehe) have been the most intense. After Gong Changhai's main force attacked Harbin without success, he led his troops to Shuangcheng. One brigade of Feng Zhanhai's troops also advanced to Heituanzi, north of Shuangcheng (seventy li from Shuangcheng), to coordinate with Gong's army. The Self-Defense Army of Yang Wenlin and Yao Bingqian is scattered around Dasanjiazi, Majiagou, and other places within fifteen li of Acheng, adopting a feint attack strategy. The approximately three thousand Japanese soldiers in Acheng have therefore dared not move. On June 17th, Gong's army advanced to Dongguansuo, forty-five li east of Shuangcheng, but was unable to advance further in one go because there were no boats to cross the Lalin River. At this time, about one brigade of puppet troops in Shuangcheng, upon hearing the news, looted extensively and retreated to Yushu, leaving the city empty. The puppet county magistrate, Wei, sent an urgent telegram to the Japanese army requesting assistance. The Japanese army then dispatched the entire main force of the Nakamura Brigade early on the 18th, heading towards Shuangcheng in two branches: one to attack Gong's army at Dongguansuo, and the other to attack Feng Zhanhai's army at Heituanzi. On the 18th, the battle at Dongguansuo broke out first, with the battle line spreading across more than ten villages. Seven Japanese planes assisted in the attack, and dozens of households in Liuxiangtun village were completely destroyed by Japanese air raids. However, Gong's army calmly responded and did not retreat at all, repeatedly charging forward. The fighting was fierce until the evening, when rain suddenly fell. On the morning of the 19th, they retreated towards Sandaogou. Feng Zhanhai's army also engaged the Japanese army in the afternoon of the 18th, suffering pressure from heavy artillery and machine guns, and losing contact with Gong's brigade. They also retreated towards Lalin. On the 21st, after the two armies reunited, they bypassed Shuangcheng and advanced towards Yushu. On the 22nd, they captured the strategic Qingshanbao, sixty li from Yushu. The Liu Yushu Brigade, the 1st Garrison Brigade of the puppet troops stationed in Yushu, was ordered to attack. Liu led his troops to the outskirts of the city but dared not advance further. Currently, Gong's brigade's cavalry has turned towards Fuyu, heading for Changchun. Li Haiqing's army, from the Anda area of Heilongjiang Province, is also advancing towards the Changchun area. The two armies are coordinating with each other, so the Japanese side has transferred cavalry from Gongzhuling to that area to block them. Li Du and Ding Chao have completed replenishing their troops in Boli. The Chen Dongshan and Ying Baobin Brigades have a total of over seven thousand troops and are currently advancing overland towards Sanxing (Yilan) via Baoqing. Japanese investigations indicate that Li has a munitions factory in Boli, producing 300,000 rounds of bullets and 10,000 artillery shells per day, with ample ammunition. Wang Delin, Gong Changhai, and Feng Zhanhai's armies are all supplied with ammunition by him. It is also reported that Li's troops, upon exiting Baoqing, will not attack immediately, but intend to contain the movement of the Japanese army's Hirose Brigade, preventing them from assisting the Japanese army in eastern Heilongjiang. It is expected that there will be no battles in that area for the time being. Wang Delin's National Salvation Army's capture of Dunhua is also to coordinate with Gong Changhai's capture of Changchun. Most of the Japanese army's Second Division is stationed in Dunhua and along the Jihui Railway. When Wang's army attacked Dunhua on the 22nd, they engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese army for a day. Wang's army eventually retreated towards Jiaohe due to a lack of bullets and is currently still confronting the nearby Japanese army. This is the situation of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers in Jilin Province over the past week. In Heilongjiang, the Japanese army, with the Amano and Hiramatsu Brigades, is advancing along the Qike Line. The Hiramatsu Brigade is advancing north from Hailun, with Baiquan and Kedong as the meeting point. Ma Zhanshan commands his troops to counterattack, and there has been fighting almost every day since June 17th. The Japanese army, unfamiliar with the geography, has been ambushed and attacked, and entire small teams have been wiped out on numerous occasions. The battle of Keshan on the 19th was particularly fierce. Ma Zhanshan personally commanded the brigades of Xu Zihe, Wu Songlin, Cai Hongyou, and Deng Wen to launch a fierce attack on Keshan. At the same time, cavalry units attacked the Japanese artillery base in Taianzhen, between Nehe and Keshan. The Japanese army's Amano Brigade, being contained in several places, could not coordinate from beginning to end. Five Japanese planes flew from Taianzhen to drop bombs, but the Black Army was scattered in the open wilderness, and the bombing was ineffective. The fierce battle lasted for sixteen hours, with the Japanese army suffering over three hundred casualties. Later, the Hiramatsu Brigade rushed to reinforce from Nahe, and the Black Army then retreated. Below Keshan, telephone communication was impossible. The Japanese army suffered from the scorching heat and the ubiquitous mud, and the soldiers all complained bitterly. Hiramatsu Brigade's artillery vehicles were stuck in Qingbeizhen north of Hailun and on the Tongken River twice on the 20th, and it took a very long time to get them out. Their supplies were also difficult to manage, so the Japanese army, having set out for many days, has not been able to achieve the effect of a pincer attack. On the 22nd, the Japanese suddenly claimed that Ma Zhanshan was hiding in a small village called Lijintun, north of Qinggang. At six o'clock in the morning, the Japanese army dispatched six fighter planes from Changchun in formation to bomb the village, dropping eighty or ninety bombs, completely destroying the entire village. Afterwards, they announced that Ma had been killed in the bombing. However, according to reliable sources, Ma has already moved to Wangkui and will cut off the Japanese army's rear lines from the Suihua area. The Japanese claim is completely false. It is also reported that Ma is now reorganizing his troops into forty independent battalions, each with three hundred to five hundred men, adopting a guerrilla warfare strategy, with no fixed departure points and fixed assembly points, making it impossible for the Japanese army to cope. Even airplanes are ineffective. Recently, in the battles north of Hailun, Ma's army has adopted this method, which has been quite effective. On the 21st, Ma's army surrounded and annihilated a Japanese reconnaissance team of officers and men north of Suihua, so the Japanese army is very afraid of Ma's army. However, the Japanese Kwantung Army headquarters is therefore planning to transfer a cavalry division to assist in the battle. (June 24th)

Chiang Kai-shek Convenes Meeting of Generals 115

Chiang to Move Office to Luojia Mountain, Hankou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang arrived in Hankou on the 28th and stayed at Yihe Village. On that day, apart from receiving He Chengjun, Xia Douyin, and Cao Haosen, he did not receive any other military and political officials. That evening, Chiang, accompanied by Cao Haosen, visited the General Headquarters and inquired about the office situation from personnel above the section chief level, encouraging them to work diligently. Late at night, he returned to the Yihe Village residence. Initially, Chiang, disliking the noise and bustle, planned to visit the new campus of Wuhan University on Luojia Mountain in Wuchang on the morning of the 29th, or establish a branch residence there to conduct office work. Upon hearing the news, the provincial government immediately rushed to make arrangements, and everything was ready that evening. A ferry was also prepared. However, at 9:00 a.m. on the 29th, Chiang visited the General Headquarters and began office work, reviewing documents and telegrams from various departments. The trip to Wuchang was temporarily canceled. At 9:30 a.m., He Chengjun, Xia Douyin, Xu Yuanquan, Wei Lihuang, Tian Zhongyao, Li Mo'an, He Jingwu, and Wang Shijie successively requested audience and were received one by one. Next, he received Huang Luchu, representative of Xu Yongchang, Huang Jun, representative of Tian Songyao, Cao Zhen, representative of Deng Xihou, and Hu Xiehuai, representative of He Jian. At noon, he returned to his residence and immediately summoned Wuhan Garrison Commander Ye Peng to inquire about the garrison situation and provide instructions. Since most of the generals were in Hankou, Chiang originally planned to convene a meeting at 4:00 p.m. on the 29th, but it was not possible due to business. It was changed to 9:00 a.m. on the 30th at the General Headquarters. Officers above the brigade commander level were summoned to attend. The final decision was made regarding the military plans for suppressing bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, and all generals were ordered not to come to Hankou unless summoned, and those in Hankou must return to their defenses within the day. It is reported that Chiang will temporarily reside in Luojia Mountain after the meeting, with a regiment from the 89th Division responsible for external defense and a battalion of Chiang's personal guards responsible for internal defense. It is also reported that He Chengjun has agreed with Chiang on the issue of military pay for the troops stationed in Hubei, and an additional 10% will be issued starting in July. Chiang has also agreed to bear the expenses for suppressing bandits from the central government, but the Sichuan troops stationed in Hubei will still be borne by the Hubei provincial government. In addition, the Hubei provincial government recently borrowed 800,000 yuan from various banks specifically for bandit suppression expenses, and the funds for repayment of principal and interest are now designated to be the income from the public bonds raised by the Qingxiang Association. (June 29th)

Pinghan Railway Reopened 116

Bandits Fleeing Southeast, Hankou Correspondence: This time, the Red bandits harassed the Pinghan Railway, and the tracks at Dongshuanghe, Liulin, Lijiazhai, Xindian, Jigongshan, Wushengguan, and Lujiashan were damaged. The damage to Lujiashan Station was particularly severe. The Red bandits numbered about ten thousand, mostly unarmed peasants. Starting on the night of June 27th, they engaged in fierce fighting with the troops of Ma Hongkui's 15th Route Army in the Lijiazhai area. On the 28th, they were still resisting stubbornly. On the 29th, the Appeasement Headquarters reported, based on Ma's telegram, that they had engaged in several hand-to-hand combats with the bandits who invaded the Dongshuanghe, Liulin, Lijiazhai, Xindian, and Jigongshan areas. Fortunately, our soldiers fought bravely, advancing one after another, and the bandits could not withstand the pressure and fled southeast across the board, and traffic has been restored. The Pinghan Railway Bureau also received a telegram from Guangshui Station stating that the troops of Wei Lihuang's 10th Division had arrived in Guangshui from Huayuan and, together with the southward troops of the 15th Route Army, were attacking the Red bandits from both sides. The remnants of the bandits were fleeing east, and all damaged tracks have been completely repaired. Therefore, the entire line can resume normal traffic. Today (29th), the special express train to the north departed from Dazhimen Station at 11:00 p.m., and the special express train to the south, which had been blocked in Xinyang, also arrived at Dazhimen Station at 6:00 p.m. today, both escorted by armored trains along the way. The train was blocked and stopped in Xinyang for a total of forty hours. All passengers are safe. After the entire line was opened, the Pinghan Railway Bureau specifically telegraphed the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the three provinces, the Appeasement Headquarters of Henan and Hubei, and the Ministry of Railways to report everything. After receiving the report, the Bandit Suppression Headquarters immediately dispatched eight aircraft from the 4th and 5th Aviation Teams to Wushengguan and the Xinyang and Bopi River areas in southern Henan to scout for bandit tracks. In the vicinity of Xinji and Wenshusi,

a large number of bandits were discovered. Eight bombs were dropped, killing many bandits. At the same time, all troops were notified to return all vehicles detained on the railway to maintain railway operations. Anyone who dares to disobey will be severely punished according to the law. Wuhu Grain Station Embezzlement and Sale of Relief Grain Case 117

Li Siyi Thrown into Jail

Public Prosecutor Initiates Prosecution

Wuhu Correspondence: In Anhui Province, there have been embezzlement cases in the accounts, previously in Bengbu in northern Anhui, and now in Wuhu in southern Anhui. The case in northern Anhui has not yet been fully used to punish the wicked, while Li Siyi, the director of the Wuhu Grain Station, has already been thrown into jail. Li successively embezzled 69 tons of relief grain, totaling 1,035 shi. He secretly sold 39 tons and 495 bags when the matter was about to end, obtaining only half the price, 1,140 yuan. When the matter was reported by the Shipping Association and various circles, Li was still very tough, relying on the strength of outsiders in the disaster relief working group. Later, as the court's summons became urgent, he voluntarily turned himself in to show that he was not afraid. Unexpectedly, the court had already investigated and confirmed the facts. As soon as Li arrived, he was not allowed bail and was detained. After repeated interrogations, the chief public prosecutor of the procuratorate, Sheng Shibi, initiated public prosecution against Li and the deputy director, Cheng Xiaoluo, and four others, each for violating Article 376, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. The reasons for the crime in the indictment are excerpted as follows: "The defendant, Li Siyi, is the director of the Wuhu Grain Station of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, Cheng Xiaoluo is the deputy director, Wu Youzhang is the accountant, Huang Xiyong is in charge of accounts, and Wang Yixuan is the warehouse manager. The defendants have committed many irregularities in the distribution of relief goods. Since the station began issuing relief grain, the weighing has been based on 2,000 pounds per ton, with 12 liang per pound, totaling 15 shi per ton according to the Cao method of measurement, which is 1,500 jin. However, according to the instructions of the working group of the committee, each pound is calculated according to the British pound, with 12.6 qian per pound, so 2,000 pounds should total 1,500 jin according to the Sima method of measurement. The Sima method of measurement is 5 jin more per 100 jin than the Cao method of measurement. The station has issued all goods according to the Cao method of measurement, so 75 jin have been embezzled per ton. In addition, the relief grain received by the station was originally calculated in large tons, but when issued, it was ordered to be changed to small tons, with a difference of about 240 pounds per ton. Due to the change in tons, they colluded with each other to cheat, resulting in a considerable amount of excess grain. In these two types of irregularities, the grain they embezzled, accumulating small amounts into large, still amounted to more than 30 tons, stored in the public grain warehouse. On a certain day last month, Li Siyi, Cheng Xiaoluo, and others discussed selling the accumulated grain to others. Yu Songzhi, who runs a shipping business, was informed of the situation by Wang Yixuan and others, and they requested Yu Songzhi to sell it on their behalf, and also invited He Xisheng of the Hede Feng Shipping Company to unload the goods, using the name of Longtan relief grain, hiring ships to transport 39 tons and 495 bags of grain, plus two bags swept from the warehouse. Yu Songzhi then sought out Shao Liangfu, a rice merchant familiar to him, told him about the relief grain, and persuaded him to purchase it, agreeing on the amount of 39 tons, with a price of 1,140 yuan, calculated at 15 shi per ton, only 2 yuan per shi, more than half the market price. Shao, greedy for profit, purchased it all and privately completed the transaction with Yu Songzhi, handing over the money to Yu to be transferred to Huang Xiyong's home. At the same time, he transferred the grain to the Zhonghefeng Warehouse, with which he was familiar, and entrusted them to sell it on his behalf at 6 yuan per shi. While they were selling, the matter was heard by the Shipping Association, and Yang Xuewu and other representatives of the Sailing Department, together with the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, went to investigate and confirmed that the grain was indeed stored there and immediately sealed it up and reported it to the court. After repeated investigations by the court, the previous situation was confirmed to be true. Li Siyi, as the director of the grain station, had previously engaged in the common embezzlement of relief goods, and this time he was the person who took the initiative to sell the relief grain, so he deserved his punishment. Cheng Xiaoluo and others jointly engaged in fraud, swallowing the money while pretending to distribute relief grain, and they are all guilty." (June 28th)

Hailstorm in Song and Lushi Counties, Henan Province 118

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Provincial Relief Association received a report from Gong Pu, the county magistrate of Song County, stating that, according to a report from Li Yanchun, the district chief of the 5th district of the county, a sudden hailstorm occurred in Checun, Sunzhuang, and other places in the district on the afternoons of June 23rd, with hailstones as large as chicken eggs and as small as plums and apricots. The wheat was shattered, the autumn seedlings were broken, and the wind and water washed everything away, leaving nothing. After surviving the calamities, they had hoped for a good wheat harvest and celebrated their recovery. However, Heaven did not pity them and sent down this great disaster. How can the surviving people bear this? Therefore, we respectfully request that you transfer funds for relief to alleviate their suffering. Upon investigation, the report is confirmed to be true. It is appropriate to forward this request for a large amount of funds to provide universal relief to the disaster victims. This would be a great act of kindness. In addition, Zhang Sijiong, chairman of the Lushi County Relief Affairs Branch, reported that the county has suffered continuous disasters and famines, and the people are struggling to eat. Heaven did not show compassion and inflicted a severe hailstorm on the 19th of this month, lasting for about two hours, with hailstones as large as fists and as small as eggs, covering the ground to a depth of one chi. More than 300 villages were destroyed, more than 200 people were killed, and all the crops were destroyed. All the grass and trees were broken. In recent years, natural disasters and man-made calamities have left the county scarred, and now it has suffered this great disaster. We lament the fate of these people. How can they survive? Therefore, we earnestly request your association to quickly allocate emergency relief to alleviate the suffering of the people. This would be a great act of kindness. It is reported that after receiving the reports from the two counties, the association immediately sent a telegram appealing to the National Relief Association and various charitable organizations to quickly provide relief funds.

Local News

Songjiang 119

Nine-County Joint Defense Conference: The county magistrate of this county, by order of the provincial government, attended the joint defense conference of Songjiang, Jinshan, Qingpu, Chengxian, Wujiang, Kunshan, Xishan, Wuxi, and Yixing counties. Previously, due to the temporary suspension of the Shanghai war, it should now be continued. It is scheduled to be held from July 1st for two days at the Wuxian County government. After receiving the document, County Magistrate Shen has already gone to Wuxian to attend.

Banning Bamboo and Wood Rafts from Occupying Waterways: The county government has repeatedly received complaints from the people that bamboo and wood businesses arbitrarily occupy the city's waterways with bamboo and wood rafts, hindering transportation and hygiene, and often causing conflicts with passing boats due to obstructing the waterways. This matter was brought to the county administration conference, which ordered a joint meeting of the Public Security Bureau's 1st District Office and the Bamboo and Wood Trade Association to discuss the ban. The interim measures for banning bamboo and wood from occupying waterways, consisting of seven articles, have now been discussed and submitted to the county government for approval before implementation. The main idea of the ban is that bamboo and wood businesses must not arbitrarily place bamboo and wood materials in places where the waterways are narrow or overflowing, hindering water transportation. If more than one-third of the river surface is occupied, it is absolutely prohibited, and the Public Security Bureau should impose penalties according to the law.

Fengxian 120

Dispute over the Educational Construction Surtax: The land tax and surtax in this county have been sufficient to cover 1% of the land price in recent years. In addition, due to war and famine, the people's strength has been depleted. Therefore, the local administrative conference for this year decided that the surtax per mu for local expenses should still be limited to 2.6 jiao, as in the previous year. However, the 8 fen per mu surtax for education is a general case. Moreover, the provincial political conference decided that the educational expenses of this county should not be discounted from the 21st year onwards. Now, the authorities are still levying it at 7 fen and 4 li, which not only violates the provincial order, but also bankrupts the entire county's education cause. Therefore, Song Zijing, director of the Education Bureau, has submitted his resignation over this issue to show his determination. At the same time, Zhou Jiushu, director of the Construction Bureau, stated that the 5 fen per mu surtax had already been allocated by the Construction Department to the South Extension Project of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Provincial Highway, and the county government had been instructed to advance 40,000 yuan to the province before it was levied, which is a pressing matter. He has telegraphed the province for instructions on the difficult situation.

Fearing Punishment for Adultery with a Hired Maid, He Flees: Feng Yougen, a farmer from Fahuaqiao, previously hired a woman surnamed Gu from Tuolin as a maid to help with farming because he was busy with farm work. Yougen, although in his fifties, was still a ladies' man. Seeing that the woman was somewhat attractive, he tried every means to seduce her and had an affair with her. Unexpectedly, the affair was discovered this spring by Feng's wife, who immediately quit on the pretext of rest. At that time, the woman was already pregnant and angrily returned home. The day before yesterday, she invited her husband, Gu Afu, to negotiate with Feng Yougen at a tea garden of a certain family in the town. Yougen also knew that he had caused trouble and fled out of fear of punishment and has not returned to this day. Therefore, Afu and others have filed a lawsuit with the county government today for legal action.

Suzhou 121

Middle School Student Commits Suicide by Drowning: Qian Linxiong, a student at Suzhou High School in Sanyuanfang, 17 years old, from Wuxi, suddenly disappeared during class yesterday afternoon. Classmates suspected that he had asked for leave. However, in the evening, a classmate went to the repair room to draw water and suddenly found Qian's body in the well. After reporting to the Discipline Office, they tried to retrieve the body, but he was already dead. There were three suicide notes in his pocket, one to his family, one to his classmates, and one to a teacher. According to his suicide notes, the reason for the suicide seemed to be that he was not making progress in his studies and had no face to live any longer. However, according to his younger brother, his brother may not have been entirely due to his studies and must have had other mental anguish, which led him to take this drastic measure. The school authorities have notified his family in Wuxi to come to Suzhou to handle the matter.

Suzhou Merchants Oppose Special Business Tax: The County Chamber of Commerce specially convened a joint meeting of various industries yesterday to discuss the issue of the provincial government's collection of special business tax. More than 120 representatives attended and resolved the following: (1) To telegraph the central government departments again, strictly ordering the provincial government to stop collecting the tax; (2) If the Jiangsu provincial government implements the special business tax, in order to maintain the central government's original plan to abolish likin and express their determination, merchants will have to stop paying all provincial taxes and telegraph both domestic and foreign authorities to request public judgment; (3) To notify the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the chambers of commerce of various counties to jointly petition the central government to order the provincial government to stop the collection; (4) To schedule a meeting again on July 2nd.

Bandits in Military Uniform Attempt to Rob Rice Mill: At around 3:00 AM on the 28th, four people wearing old gray military uniforms and carrying box guns and flashlights suddenly appeared at the Daxing Rice Mill on Nanheyan outside the West Gate of Wuyi. Important News on Education

Reasons for the Turmoil at National Central University 132

The turmoil at National Central University (NCU) involving the rejection of President Duan and the government's dissolution of the university were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Here is a summary of the causes of this turmoil, based on information gathered during investigations.

Motives for the Turmoil 133

Since the abolition of the university district system, the funding for NCU has been fundamentally shaken, and the anxiety of teachers and students throughout the university has been growing for some time. Last autumn, after the Jiangsu Provincial Party and Government Joint Conference decided to suspend the allocation of funds to NCU at the request of primary and secondary school principals in Jiangsu Province, the students of the university repeatedly petitioned the government to secure the university's funding. This dragged on until now without any results. After the Shanghai-Songhu Battle, various sources of funding dried up, and most of the university's professors sought other employment to maintain their livelihoods. By April, faculty and staff were only receiving 30% of their salaries, which was hardly enough to live on given the high cost of living in the capital. This is why the faculty association repeatedly held meetings to discuss ways to secure salaries and even organized a one-day strike. The students, facing difficulties in raising funds after the Shanghai-Songhu Battle, requested that the university allow them to register and attend classes first, deferring the payment of fees, with professors acting as guarantors and repayments made in installments. Seeing the accumulating arrears in professors' salaries and the university's shrinking funds, the students naturally sympathized with the faculty. As a result, faculty and students jointly formed a Financial Independence Movement Committee, requesting the government to use the interest from the British Boxer Indemnity as the NCU fund. The government refused, citing that the Boxer Indemnity's use was stipulated in an exchange of notes and could not be changed. The students' demands were not met, and resentment grew. It was unavoidable that emotions would run high. Therefore, the motive for the turmoil at NCU was essentially financial. If the funding issue could be guaranteed, the problem of the president could be tolerated and resolved, and there would not have been the beating and rejection of Duan as acting president.

The Appointment of Duan as Acting President 134

Before a formal president was appointed at NCU, Liu Guanghua was acting president. Liu left the university a week ago due to unfavorable circumstances. Those who were opposed and left the university before him included Liu Yunchou, Dean of the College of Agriculture (when Liu left, the students of the College of Agriculture held a farewell party, and the professors advocated retaining him, resulting in a strike that has not yet been resolved), Yang Gongda, Dean of the College of Law, Fang Guangqi, Head of the Department of Physics, and others. After Liu left, Yi Qian took over his duties, but Liu's departure was not official, and Yi was acting without the actual authority to handle university affairs. In reality, it was difficult for Liu to return to the university, and the position of the president could not remain vacant for long. Therefore, Duan was appointed as acting president and came to the university.

Reasons for Student Rejection of Duan 135

When Zhu Jiahua took over as president of NCU, it was after a period of turmoil at the university. The government was deeply concerned about the complexity of the student body. After Zhu took office, he expelled several students to rectify the academic atmosphere and frequently rejected student requests, resulting in strained relations with the students. I recall that last autumn, when students requested the government to approve Zhu's resignation, a student representative told a reporter, "We believe that if President Zhu goes to the political arena to develop, his achievements will certainly be more significant than running NCU well." The implicit meaning was clear. During the faculty association's investigation of the accounting records due to the lack of salary payments, it was discovered that Zhu had misappropriated more than 30,000 yuan of disaster relief donations during his tenure to pay the salaries of faculty and staff who had left their positions with Zhu. This aroused public outrage. Therefore, at the general student meeting on the 27th, it was decided to send a letter to Zhu, demanding that he return the 30,000 yuan of disaster relief donations within three days and requesting the government to punish him. Yesterday, when the students heard the news that Duan Xipeng was acting president, they believed that Duan was Zhu's replacement and expressed their dissatisfaction. They decided to hold another general assembly the next day to discuss methods to reject Duan. At 8:00 AM on the 29th, while they were meeting in the gymnasium, someone saw Duan's Ministry of Education car parked downstairs in the president's office. They rushed to report to the assembly that Duan had arrived at the university. The assembly stormed out of the gymnasium and headed to the president's office to confront Duan. Sha Menghai, the secretary of the Ministry of Education who had come with Duan, had already taken the opportunity to escape. Duan, seeing that the students were yelling and about to hit him, raised his arms to grab the yellers. The other students took offense on their behalf and began to act, resulting in Duan being severely beaten. According to students who witnessed the incident, if Duan had retreated upon seeing the situation, the beating would not have occurred. Even after the beating started, if Duan had not grabbed people, he would not have been injured so severely. Therefore, after thoroughly investigating the reason for the students' rejection of Duan, it was simply to vent their anger at Zhu through Duan. Duan was confident that he had no ill will towards the students, so he did not think and went to the university abruptly, resulting in the misfortune.

Duan Xipeng's Report 136

Here is Duan's report to the Executive Yuan and the injury report issued by doctor Weng Zhilong.

Report regarding the matter of submitting a report: I respectfully received the instructions from your esteemed Yuan to temporarily assume the position of President of National Central University and to go to the university to take office on the same day. Upon receiving this, I respectfully complied and went to the university at 8:30 this morning. After discussing the matter with Provost Cha Jiao for a moment in the president's office, the students of the university came from the gymnasium where they were holding a meeting, making a lot of noise. They barged into the president's office and forced me to go to the gymnasium to see them. I thought that the students of the university might not yet understand the government's painstaking efforts in appointing an acting president. I specifically asked to send a few representatives to meet with me first. But before I could finish speaking, a group of students forcibly dragged me downstairs, twisting, pulling, and beating me along the way, until they reached the outside of the South Gaoyuan Gate, where they kicked me to the ground, raining blows of fists and feet on me. My long gown was torn to shreds, and the car I rode in was also smashed. In the 45th meeting of your esteemed Yuan, it was resolved to appoint me as the acting president of National Central University. At that time, I had stated that National Central University is the highest institution of learning in the country, and we must carefully select a person of virtue and reputation and with educational experience as the president. I judged myself to be unworthy of this important task and repeatedly declined. Later, your esteemed Yuan stated that finding a candidate for president could not be done in a short time. Now that the summer vacation is approaching, various university affairs, such as hiring professors and handling admissions, urgently need someone to take charge to avoid delays. I was compelled to comply with the utmost intention of your esteemed Yuan to maintain National Central University, to fulfill my duties to the best of my ability, and to apply for a temporary appointment to avoid fault. Unexpectedly, this morning, upon my compliance with the order, a group of students acted with such violence. I was appointed without merit and I am filled with dread. I respectfully submit the situation of my being beaten at Central University today for your esteemed review and decision. Respectfully submitted to the President of the Executive Yuan, Wang.

Weng Zhilong's Report on Duan's Injuries 137

Lacerated contusion and bleeding wound on the left wrist, with a diameter of 8 points and a depth of 2 points; Contusion, swelling, redness, and pain on the top of the right head; Bleeding from a small oblique wound on the right forehead; Small bleeding from the skin and flesh of the left ear; Lacerated contusion on the right lower leg, with a diameter of 2 points; Minor skin wound on the right hand; Contusion, swelling, and pain on both shoulders; Contusion, swelling, and pain on the left and right sides of the upper back.

Zhu's Resignation Letter 138

The original text of the resignation letter submitted by Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua to the Executive Yuan is recorded below: Regarding the matter of submitting a request to resign, Jiahua's virtue is thin and his ability is lacking, and his handling has been flawed, leading to the event this morning in which Duan, the acting vice-minister and acting president of National Central University, was besieged and injured by students. The acting president went to the university to take office this morning. Before he could speak, hundreds of students gathered at the president's office, shouting and hitting. The situation led to serious injuries, and the acting president has submitted a report on the injuries on record. In recent years, academic atmosphere has become unruly, and there are also malicious people fanning the flames, intending to disrupt the overall situation and shake the foundation of the country. This is like a fire spreading across the prairie, and it is difficult to control. Jiahua is aware of his shortcomings, and a broken cauldron is always ominous. Therefore, after clearly issuing the order in late December last year, he hesitated again and again and dared not take office. Later, the national crisis became more urgent, and it was morally impossible to decline. He reluctantly assumed the difficult task, hoping to serve for a few months, but failed to retire bravely, thus creating trouble. Continuing in this way will only add to the blame. Therefore, I hereby submit my resignation to avoid hindering the virtuous path, humbly requesting your immediate approval, so that I can fulfill my original intention, and I await your orders with utmost humility.

Local News

Municipal Bureau of Education Orders Senior High Schools and Above to Implement Summer Military Training 140

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a directive to senior high schools and above in this city, stating that on June 27th, the Ministry of Education sent a quick postal telegram stating that the Training Supervision Department sent a telegram stating that the amended plan for military education in senior high schools and above stipulates that continuous and strict military training should be implemented every year during the summer vacation. During this time of national crisis, it is urgent to implement this plan to enhance international capabilities. In addition to ordering military instructors in various schools to comply, this special telegram is sent to request the education administrative agencies and schools to strictly implement this plan, and not allow anyone to make excuses to postpone or stop it. This is in the interest of public amity. In addition, it was approved to implement three weeks of extremely strict military training during the summer vacation, which is stipulated in the revised plan for military education in senior high schools and above. During this time of national crisis, it is especially important to strictly comply with this plan. The approval was granted, and in addition to issuing separate orders, this urgent order is sent to the schools to comply with and implement this plan and not to make excuses to postpone it. Students who have not received this strict military training should also comply with Article 6 of the National Physical Education Law. On the same day, the Ministry of Education also sent a telegram stating that the Shandong Provincial Department of Education sent a telegram stating that the Training Supervision Department sent a telegram ordering senior high schools and above to strictly implement summer military training. It was noted that schools are closed during the summer vacation according to regulations, and students must also leave school. The Shandong Provincial Education Department asked for instructions on how this training should be implemented, and the reply was that "students undergoing military training should be ordered to stay at the school to continue the three weeks of training according to the planned schedule after the examinations of this academic year are completed, and should comply with the Ministry of Education's telegram." In addition to issuing separate orders, this urgent order is sent to the schools for compliance.

Records of Temple Bell Striking (39) 155

—Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu (pen name)

43. The whole village was in an uproar. Mr. Zhu called me out to see what was happening.

"Bandits are coming to loot, go and take a look." Little Erge said to me on the road. I squeezed through the crowd and saw a strange piece of paper pasted on the wall of the earth god temple. It was written:

"Commander Zhao Fei of the National Revolutionary Army's Thirteenth Division orders Zhang Huzi to send 5,000 yuan to Lake Muzhi today to reward the troops. We have not received pay for five months. If you have the heart to sit and watch us starve to death, then you are an inhumane miser. You are given three days to send the money, using a flashlight as a signal. If the deadline passes without the money, don't blame me for turning ruthless, so be it."

Can you guess what this note was pasted with? No one would easily guess. It was pasted with mud. Isn't that interesting? Zhang Huzi woke up from his dream in Yixia Cave. I saw him running around in a panic in the sunlight for the first time to ask for information. What could he do? His family property was almost eaten up. After running around for three days, he couldn't even raise 500 yuan, so he had to move his whole family to the city to hide. From then on, he never went back to the countryside. On the morning of the fourth day, another note was posted in front of the earth god temple, even more severe than the last one.

"Commander Zhao Fei of the National Revolutionary Army's Thirteenth Division again orders Zhang Huzi. You disobey the orders of this division commander, which is extremely hateful. You are again given three days to contribute 10,000 yuan. If you fail again, I will kill your entire family and friends, leaving no one alive, so be it."

For the past few days, every villager has been alarmed. There are more than twenty families with guns, but everyone is just protecting themselves, without any organization, just waiting for the bandits to come and disarm them. We have asked the security team a dozen times, but none of them are willing to come. The few of us in the ancient temple, however, are sleeping soundly. If the bandits come, we will invite them to drink two cups of clear water. If they want to eat coarse rice, we can also offer them a big pot. If they like rags and worn-out cotton, we can also give them away. Little Brother and I are still worried about being kidnapped. Mr. Zhu said, "It would be good to be kidnapped and try out bandit education." These are our plans during tea breaks.

On the fifth day, news came that a five-year-old child five miles away from the ancient temple had been killed by bandits after being kidnapped for ransom. The child's father was an old farmer who farmed his own land. After the bandits kidnapped him, they demanded 800 yuan. The old farmer mortgaged his land and sold his house to raise 400 yuan. The bandits took the silver and pointed to a small mound of earth, saying, "Do you want your child? He's in that mound."

Mr. Zhu went to the city in anger. What did he go to do? Unfortunately, there was no time to ask before Old Xu spread rumors, saying, "Mr. Zhu is afraid of being kidnapped by bandits, so he ran away."

Local News

Careless Handling of Bombs Causes Tragedy 156

Moved from Zhabei to the Arsenal

Shell Explodes, Killing Three and Injuring Two

When the Japanese army withdrew, they left behind many hand-pulled grenades, shells, and bombs in Zhabei, Wusongjiang Bay, and other places. After our side took over, we immediately issued a notice and tried to find and collect the bombs, concentrating them in the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau. Subsequently, personnel from the arsenal were dispatched to inspect them, load them, and store them in the arsenal's armory. Yesterday, before the arsenal had inspected them, the Zhabei Office hired movers' trucks to transport a large number of collected hand-pulled grenades, shells, bombs, etc., to the arsenal. When they arrived at the arsenal and were being moved into the warehouse, a worker was careless and dropped one, causing it to explode, killing two people and injuring three. The details are as follows:

Shell Explosion: Yesterday afternoon at about 1:00 PM, the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau hired a large truck from the China Moving Company, with four moving workers on board. They loaded many hand-pulled grenades, bombs, shells, etc., inside. The loading was completed at about 2:00 PM, and then Deputy Officer Hong Shuren was dispatched to escort the truck, which entered the South City via Zhongshan Road. At 3:00 PM, they arrived at the No. 13 warehouse of the West Fort Armory of the arsenal and notified Zhang Zulian, the armory chief. At the same time, the moving workers, together with the old warehouse soldiers Gan Wanyou, Gao Defu, Chen Zhengxiang, etc., moved the items from the truck to the No. 13 warehouse for storage. After only a dozen or so items had been moved, the moving worker Gu Shan suddenly dropped a steel shell weighing about twenty pounds at the entrance of the warehouse. The detonator on the shell had not been removed, and upon impact, it immediately exploded.

Casualties: The worker and the escorting officer, Hong Shuren, were killed on the spot, their flesh and blood scattered, a truly tragic sight. The explosion also injured the armory soldiers Gan Wanyou, Gao Shangde, and Chen Zhengxiang who were also moving the items. Gao's legs were blown off, and Chen's head and one leg were also destroyed, resulting in extremely serious injuries. Only Gan's injuries were relatively minor. The time was 3:15 PM.

Sent to Hospital for Treatment: When the shell exploded, there was a lot of smoke. The arsenal, unable to immediately determine the truth, suspected it was due to carelessness and immediately telegraphed all the fire brigades. Upon hearing the news, the fire brigades from various districts immediately dispatched fire trucks to the West Fort. As there was no spreading fire, they immediately used the fire brigade's ambulances to send the injured warehouse soldiers Gan Wanyou, Gao Shangde, and Chen Zhengxiang to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment.

Brief History of the Casualties: Those killed on the spot yesterday were Hong Shuren, deputy officer of the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau, 25 years old, from Guangdong. He previously served as a deputy officer in the police regiment and as a special agent in the police brigade headquarters. When the Zhabei Office was established, he was transferred by Director Huang to serve in the office. Gu Shan, from Tongzhou, Jiangbei, in his twenties, was a moving worker at the China Moving Company. The seriously injured were Chen Zhengxiang and Gao Shangde, and the injured was Gan Wanyou. All three were from Jiangbei and had been serving as warehouse soldiers in the arsenal for more than ten years. They were extremely careful when handling munitions and had never had an accident. Yesterday, when the explosion occurred, their backs were close to the explosion site, resulting in serious injuries.

Dispatch of Personnel for Investigation: After the accident, the arsenal immediately telephoned the Zhabei Office and the Municipal Government. After receiving the call, the office immediately dispatched two service personnel, Huang He and Zhou Dexin, to the arsenal to investigate the truth of the accident. After arriving at the arsenal, Huang and Zhou met with the armory chief Zhang Zulian and also visited Director Song to ask for instructions regarding the matter. They returned at about 5:00 PM.

Aftermath Issues: The bodies of Hong Shuren and Gu Shan, who were killed, are still placed opposite the No. 13 warehouse at the West Fort, covered with reed mats. The office will collect the bodies today. As for the injured Gan, Gao, and Chen, Gao and Chen are critically injured and their lives are in danger, so there is little hope. Yesterday, the general affairs department of the arsenal first issued each person ten yuan for transportation. If they die from their injuries, they will be treated as a case of death in the line of duty and given preferential compensation. The issue of compensation will be negotiated with the Municipal Government. Gao also died last night due to his serious injuries.

Armory Chief's Statement: According to Mr. Zhang Zulian, the armory chief of the arsenal, this incident was extremely unfortunate. After the takeover committee took over various places, the arsenal agreed with the Municipal Government that the Public Security Bureau would be responsible for (1) collecting and (2) storing all the munitions left in the withdrawn areas, and then the arsenal would be responsible for (1) inspecting and (2) transporting them to eliminate the danger. The bombs, etc., transported by the Zhabei Office today had not been inspected by the arsenal and were transported by workers hired by the moving company, who had no experience and were unaware of the danger, resulting in such a major accident due to carelessness. Furthermore, since the accident yesterday, the driver of the truck, because there were still munitions left to be moved, did not dare to drive the truck away, so the truck that transported the items last night is still parked at the accident site at the West Fort.

British Warship Runs Aground in Yangtze River 157

Hidden Reef at Huangshizui Causes Accident

Fortunately, All Crew Members Are Safe

Recently, merchant ships have been having accidents one after another, and even more ships have been having accidents on the Yangtze River due to the rapid rise of the river. Now, there is another incident of a British Yangtze River warship running aground and being damaged downstream of Chongqing. After a detailed investigation by our reporter, the report is as follows:

Wrong Navigation Channel: In recent years, the British Navy has increased the number of warships on the Yangtze River to protect merchant ships because of frequent bandit alarms on the Yangtze River and frequent attacks by communist bandits on merchant ships in various places upstream, especially those of British merchants. The gunboat HMS Peterel, which specializes in escorting ships on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, was sailing downstream from Chongqing. One day, when it was sailing 140 nautical miles downstream of Chongqing in an area called Ping'an River, it encountered rising water. The navigator mistook the channel, resulting in the major accident of running aground. The rivers in Sichuan have many hidden reefs, making navigation extremely difficult. Once they are submerged by rising water, it is even more difficult to see them. A little carelessness can lead to running aground.

Grounding and Impact: The HMS Peterel warship mistakenly sailed into the Huangshizui hidden reef in the Ping'an River area. The front of the ship rammed into the reef, and the bottom of the bow entered the reef. It was too late to reverse and pull out. The bottom of the bow had already been breached, and river water rushed in. In a short time, the water was eight feet deep. At that time, the ship was sailing downstream with the rapid current, making the speed even greater. When it reached Huangshizui, the bow of the ship crashed violently into the large reef in front, causing excessive vibration. After this collision, the head was damaged by as much as sixteen or seventeen feet, and the front of the bow was completely damaged.

Stranding and Rescue: After the accident, the captain sent a telegram for help. Fearing that the river water would flood the other compartments and sink the ship to the bottom of the river, he urgently drove the entire ship completely onto the shallow beach, stranding the entire ship to prevent it from sinking immediately. The captain then used cement and wooden boards to first patch the broken hole under the bow and then pumped out the water from the compartments to float the ship. At that time, he ordered a British gunboat in the upper reaches to tow the ship out of the shallows and bring it to Shanghai for repairs.

Damage Report: It is reported that the bow of the British warship was destroyed and the ship was damaged in almost a quarter of its parts. Although the bottom of the ship was temporarily repaired, it must be rebuilt in the dry dock. The bow that was struck must also be rebuilt in Shanghai. The total loss from the warship running aground this time is at least sixty or seventy thousand yuan. It is currently being repaired and towed, and will soon be sent to Shanghai for major repairs at the shipyard. Fortunately, no crew members were injured, but the structures at the front of the bow were completely destroyed.

No Definite Date for Japanese Troop Withdrawal from D District 158

According to the Central News Agency, after repeated negotiations by our members of the Joint Commission, Yu Hongjun and Wen Yingxing, with the Japanese side regarding the withdrawal of Japanese troops from D District, there has been no definitive response. Committee member Yu Hongjun had no choice but to send a letter to Mr. Kennett, chairman of the Joint Commission, on the 28th of last month, urging the Japanese side to withdraw as soon as possible. However, as of last night, the Japanese side had not notified the Joint Commission and our side of a definite date for the withdrawal. The Japanese naval authorities in Shanghai sent personnel to visit Committee member Yu Hongjun a few days ago, stating that the Japanese troops in D District could withdraw in the shortest possible time, but there was still no definite date. Committee member Yu replied that our side had already submitted this matter to the Joint Commission for negotiation and asked them to discuss it with the Joint Commission.

Jiang Zuobin Speaks 159

Minimum Requirements for Resolving the Liaoning Case

Restoration of Sino-Russian Diplomatic Relations to Be Handled by Mo

On the 28th of last month, a local English-language evening newspaper reported that a senior official of the National Government, at the request of the League of Nations Investigating Committee, drafted a new plan for resolving the Liaoning case at the Guling Conference. Such a bizarre story naturally cannot be believed by us. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency specifically visited Jiang Zuobin, chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee and ambassador to Japan, at his private residence yesterday to inquire about this matter. According to Jiang, this matter is absolutely untrue, and there is absolutely no such thing. As far as I (Jiang referring to himself) know, the Investigating Committee needs to solicit opinions from both the Chinese and Japanese governments to draft a report. Therefore, after arriving in Peiping, the committee inquired with our side about the minimum requirements for resolving the Northeast issue. Our side responded based on the principle of not hindering the integrity of China's territory and administrative power, and there was no so-called new plan. I dare say that no matter how foolish the people in the government are, they would not have proposed such an opinion. As for the restoration of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations, when I was in Beijing, I heard that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs had telegraphed Mo Dehui, the representative to Russia who was recuperating in Italy, to return to his post to handle the matter. He should have already returned to Russia now.

Rumors of the Death of a Russian Prisoner Turned Into a Missing Persons Case 160

Brother of the Deceased Bases Report on Three Russians

But the Three Russians Deny Everything

French Police Prepare Coffin for Examination Today

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, the case of the disappearance of the Russian Grantzki has been widely publicized in this city. After the Second Special District District Court announced the facts of the case a few days ago, the case has become clear. However, what is still unclear is whether the missing Russian Grantzki is the same person as George Radikiev. The court was unable to confirm whether they were the same person because the police report was written in Chinese. A reporter from the Hua Dong News Agency went to the Lujiawan Police Station yesterday to investigate. According to a senior police officer at the police station, the Russian George Radikiev who died of illness was actually Grantzki. The police station is currently investigating this error and is unwilling to make any comments before obtaining sufficient evidence. However, according to reliable information obtained by a reporter from the Hua Dong News Agency, the police have already summoned four Russians who are related to the case. Two of the four Russians were the ones who were sentenced to seven days of detention at the same time as George Radikiev, as reported yesterday. Another one was also one of those who were sentenced to detention. Another person was the brother of the deceased who reported the case. The reason for this is that the brother of the deceased had received reports from the aforementioned three Russians that before his death, they had witnessed the deceased being subjected to extrajudicial punishment in prison, bleeding from the chest, and then disappearing. The brother of the deceased then reported the case based on this information. However, when the police questioned the three Russians, all three of them completely denied making such a statement. As a result, the brother of the deceased was very embarrassed and declared to the police station that when the three of them made this report, two friends were present, so he asked the police station to summon these two people to testify. It is still difficult to know the final result of the police's investigation into this matter. However, the Second Special District District Court also released a new piece of evidence yesterday, stating that two days after the Russian George Radikiev died of illness, the police lawyer Gu Shouxi, accompanied by a Russian, went to request the release of the body. At that time, the inspection office, because the police report stated that the deceased had no family, wife, or occupation, and now someone claimed to be his brother, expressed suspicion and ordered that a written request be submitted before it could be approved. At that time, the reasons for requiring a written request were also explained. The Russian listened to the explanation and then left, but he has not submitted a written request to this day. Therefore, the rumors that have arisen may be related to the Russian or may have other background involved. Yesterday, the chief clerk of the Second Special District Court, Xiao, also told a reporter from the Hua Dong News Agency that the court only knew of a Russian prisoner named George Radikiev and that there was absolutely no one named Grantzki. Even if the two were the same person, and the rumors about the cause of his death were indeed suspicious, the court's official pronouncements and examinations by the prosecutor Wu and the forensic doctor Wei were still in place and could serve as evidence. If outsiders still believe that this is not enough, then they can have the body of the prisoner exhumed and re-examined to quell the rumors from the outside world. The court authorities will now decide how to deal with the rumor-mongers according to the law after the police have completed their investigation. Yesterday, Deputy Inspector Pauldy of the Western Branch of the French General Police Department, accompanied by Chinese Detective Qin Youyu, went to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch to notify them to hire a gasoline boat today with the branch's personnel to go to the Tangwan Cemetery to exhume the coffin of George Radikiev and bring it to Shanghai to be sent to the autopsy room of the Municipal Council Hospital on Thales Road for a doctor to open the coffin and re-examine the body.

삼문만 시찰기 (2) 161

기업 회사들이 잇따라 투자하다

화교들은 원대한 계획을 세우려고 하다

삼문만의 현황: 태안함은 석포에서 3시간 항해하여 삼문만 내의 해유항에 도착했습니다. 겹겹이 쌓인 산과 푸른 파도는 잔잔하여 경치가 뛰어나고 독보적이라고 할 만합니다. 시찰단은 함선에서 내려 작은 배로 갈아타고 상륙했습니다. 당시에는 큰 비가 쏟아지고 길이 질척거렸습니다. 시찰단은 관부 지역을 일주하며 옷과 신발이 모두 젖었습니다. 길을 따라 밭이 가로세로로 뻗어 있어 끝이 보이지 않아 토지가 비옥하고 농작물이 풍성할 것으로 예상됩니다. 또한 순검사에 이르러 허정좌가 세운 부두와 삼문만 여관을 참관했습니다. 인근에는 보안대 1개 소대가 주둔하고 있고, 향민들은 편안하게 생업에 종사하고 있으니 진실로 도원선경입니다. 11시에 함선으로 돌아와 만내의 악정양으로 다시 출발하여 제방 축조 공사를 시찰했습니다. 오후 5시에 삼문만을 떠나 다시 석포로 돌아왔고, 시찰 임무는 여기서 끝났습니다. 태안함은 석포에서 태풍을 피하기 위해 하룻밤 정박했고, 27일 새벽 4시에 닻을 올려 보타로 유람을 갔습니다. 29일에는 용륜을 타고 상해로 돌아왔습니다. 삼문만 전체 면적은 매우 넓고, 만내의 항만은 복잡하게 나뉘어 있으며, 섬들이 흩어져 있습니다. 토질은 비옥하고 물산은 풍부하며, 수륙 교통 모두 편리합니다. 만 전체 주민은 총 7만 5천여 호이고, 인구는 약 37만 명입니다. 만약 개항 이후 상업이 번성하면 5백만 명 이상을 수용할 수 있을 것입니다. 주민들은 육지에서는 제염과 농업을 주로 하고, 해안에서는 어업과 상업을 생업으로 삼습니다. 만 전체는 어염이 주요 산출물입니다. 어업에 있어서는 춘추 양 계절의 수익이 약 80여만 원에 달할 수 있습니다. 과학적인 방법을 더하여 점차적으로 개선하면 그 수익을 10배로 늘릴 수 있을 것입니다. 소금은 항구를 따라 바닷물을 끓여 소금을 만드는 사람이 약 3천여 호이며, 계절마다 750만 섬을 수확합니다. 게다가 소금의 품질은 희고 깨끗하며 맛이 좋습니다. 다른 물산도 모두 갖추어져 있습니다. 식물로는 소나무, 삼나무, 대나무, 상수리나무, 잡목이 있고, 벼, 삼, 면화, 콩류, 보리, 밀, 땅콩, 담배, 차, 동유, 생칠, 쪽 등이 있습니다. 광물로는 은, 알루미늄, 철, 주석, 안티몬, 망간, 석탄, 자석, 청석, 형석 등이 있습니다. 만내의 기후는 온화하며, 여름에는 상해보다 10도 낮아 피서에 매우 적합합니다. 겨울에는 산으로 둘러싸여 있어 해풍이 들어오지 않아 오히려 상해보다 10도 높습니다. 여름에는 몹시 덥지 않고 겨울에는 눈이 쌓이지 않습니다. 만내의 수량은 깊이가 일정하지 않으며, 가장 깊은 곳은 사반양 일대인데, 깊이가 20여 길에 달합니다. 만 톤 이상의 윤선도 사반양 양안에 정박할 수 있습니다. 만구에는 어산이 있고, 위에는 등대가 있어 남양 민광 각 부에서 상해 천진으로 항행하는 표적이 됩니다. 이 산의 서쪽으로 북행하면 석포 정해 영파 등지로 통하고, 상해로 돌아갑니다. 만의 북쪽은 악정, 호진, 차원, 백교 등의 항구로, 만의 서쪽은 기문, 해유, 건도 등의 항구로, 모두 내륙 각지로 통하는 요충지입니다. 육로 교통은 해유항 관부 지역에서 서쪽으로 해유진까지 이르고, 이는 유천태로 가는 필수 경로입니다. 북쪽으로는 영해에 달하고, 봉화에 이르러 영파로 통합니다. 서쪽으로는 천태와 연결되고, 북쪽으로는 신창에 이르러 승현, 조아를 거쳐 소흥에 이릅니다. 전당강을 건너면 항주에 도착할 수 있습니다. 남쪽으로는 황암, 낙청에 이르러 온주로 통합니다. 서쪽으로는 동양, 의오에 이르러 항강 철도와 연결되어 완강으로 통할 수 있습니다. 최근 절강성 정부는 해유항 남안을 따라 삼의 장거리 자동차 도로를 건설하여 항강 철도와 연결할 계획인데, 그러면 하루 만에 항주에 도착할 수 있어 교통이 더욱 편리해질 것입니다. 삼문만의 형세, 물산, 교통을 보면 우리나라 해강의 유일한 요항이라고 할 만합니다. 정부와 국민이 합심하여 경영하여 성공한다면 대련 청도가 독점할 수 없을 뿐만 아니라 국가 경제와 국민 생활에도 막대한 도움이 될 것입니다.

개척 계획의 일면: 국민정부 및 절강성 정부 회감위원이 지정한 바에 따라 해유항을 삼문만의 중심 상항으로 삼고, 항구 남안을 따라 삼의 장거리 자동차 도로를 건설하여 항강 철도와 연결하고, 절강, 안휘, 강서 3성을 관통하고, 북쪽으로는 호진, 남쪽으로는 민월에 통하게 하여 수도 중추에 적합하게 한다. 보오에서 묘두산 일대를 상업 지역으로 획정하고, 순검사 오산 화서를 시정 중심으로 삼는다. 항구를 따라 윤선 부두를 건설하고, 시정부는 첨갱당에 설치하고, 공안국은 오산에 설치하고, 수경국은 소도산에 설치할 계획이다. 현재 보안대는 순검사에 주둔하고, 보호대는 화시가에 주둔하고 있다. 해유 일대의 토지는 모두 만 톤 이상의 윤선을 정박할 수 있는 부두를 건설할 수 있다. 묘두산 해안은 사탄이므로 해수욕장을 건설하기로 규정했다. 해유항의 북쪽 정서항의 남쪽은 주택 지역으로 획정하고, 정서항의 북쪽 기문항의 남쪽은 지세가 좁고 길어 조선소를 건설하는 데 가장 적합하다. 기문항의 북쪽은 호진항에 이르기까지 농간 지역 및 공장 지역으로 한다. 호진항의 동쪽 사반양의 동북쪽은 피서 지역 및 수륙 비행장으로 획정한다. 악정양의 서쪽 및 만어양의 북쪽은 모두 제염 지역으로 획정한다. 사반양 만산양 사이의 여러 작은 섬은 모두 어항으로 획정한다.

40인 협동조합: 해유항 남안의 상업 지역에는 이미 도남척식회사가 아름다운 숙지 수천 무를 매입했고, 신형회사는 이미 사반양 연안 가장 깊은 곳 일대의 토지를 매입하여 외양 거륜이 정박할 수 있는 부두를 축조할 계획이다. 최근에는 흥업회사도 대량의 지산을 매입하여 벽돌 공장, 정제 소금 공장, 정미소, 제재소 및 흥업 상업 지구 등을 건설할 계획이다. 영전회사는 연와산에 조림장을 건설할 계획이다. 이 외에도 개인과 남양 화교들도 이미 오산촌 남쪽 일대의 지방을 매입하여 주택을 건축하고 공장을 설립할 계획이다. 따라서 그곳의 수용지 가격은 1무당 100원 이상이고, 염전의 땅은 1무당 300원이다. 또한 상인 허정좌는 자금을 모아 삼문만 순검사 부근에 땅을 매입하여 부두를 축조하고, 창고를 설치하고, 여관을 건설하고, 상점을 열고, 익리 상륜을 창업하여 상해에서 삼문만으로 운행하여 교통을 편리하게 한다. 최근에는 서신부 주내식 등이 40인 협동조합을 발기하여 여러 사람의 지혜를 모으고 여러 사람이 들면 쉬워진다는 것을 실현하고자 한다. 그 방법은 각자 2,500원을 납입하여 40명이 합쳐 10만 원을 만들고, 이 10만 원의 기금으로 도남척식회사에서 숙지 1천 무를 매입하고, 상업 지구를 개척하기 전에 이 여러 해 동안 경작한 숙지를 오로지 과일과 채소 2가지 품목만 심는다. 들리는 바에 따르면 3, 5년 안에 원가를 회수할 수 있다고 한다. 그 방법은 매우 좋다. 만약 우리나라 사람들이 약간의 소단체를 모아 소수의 자본을 투입하여 생산이 풍부하고 이익이 막대한 사업을 한다면 삼문만의 발전은 눈 깜짝할 사이에 이루어질 것이다. 들리는 바에 따르면 40인 협동조합이 이미 설립되었고, 화교 건설위원회 방면에서도 원대한 계획을 세우려고 하고, 웅후한 자본을 조달하여 삼문만을 열심히 개발하려고 한다. 바라건대 정부 당국은 더 이상 공론만 일삼고 좋은 항구를 황폐하게 내버려두지 말고, 속히 재정적 준비를 하여 힘써 실행을 도모하고, 위아래가 합심하고, 여러 사람이 들면 쉬워진다면 삼문만의 개척은 상당한 연월 안에 성과를 거둘 수 있을 것이다. (완)

제사 공장 파업 확산 165

閘北구 15개 공장 완전 가입

당정 기관 어제 대책 협의

오늘 오후 우선 소환 조사 예정

虹口구 怡昌 제사 공장 노동자 파업 이후 파업 노동자들이 각 공장으로 몰려가 일치된 행동을 강요한 결과 云成, 祥成, 通纬, 裕经, 新论, 厚福, 纬纶, 第七 제사 공장이 계속 파업에 들어갔고 统益, 仁记 제사 공장은 파급을 피하기 위해 자진 휴업에 들어갔다. 이에 虹口구 제사 공장은 완전 마비되었다. 시 공안국 5구 3분소는 보호를 위해 여전히 경찰을 증파하여 각 공장에 주둔시켜 경계를 강화했다. 전날 저녁 파업 노동자들은 임금 문제가 시 전체 제사 공장과 관련된 문제라고 여겨 수십 명을 모아 閘北구로 몰려가 작업을 저지하려 했으나 5구 3분 소장의 경찰이 권유했으나 효과가 없었다.

파업이 閘北으로 확산: 시 공안국 4구 경찰서는 보고를 받고 즉시 경찰을 증파하여 설득을 시도했다. 그러나 파업 노동자들은 이미 무리를 지어 閘北구 交通西路 丰泰, 慎记 등의 제사 공장으로 몰려갔다. 경찰이 극력 설득하고 경찰을 증파하여 보호했음에도 불구하고 여공들은 원래 겁이 많아 극도로 당황하여 질서가 혼란스러워 자진하여 물러나와 일할 마음이 없었다. 각 공장은 어쩔 수 없이 조기 퇴근시켜 기계 손상을 방지했다. 오후 5시가 되자 閘北구 久丰, 鼎记, 协记, 源和, 力昌泰 등도 잇따라 휴업에 들어갔다.

어제 아침 全停: 어제 아침부터 閘北구 전체 제사 공장, 예를 들어 潭子灣 丰余记 제사기 200대, 中与略久记 제사기 170대, 交通西路 丰泰慎记 제사기 416대, 沪大路 复昌 제사기 416대, 柳营路 和记 제사기 228대, 广肇路 源记 제사기 480대, 长安路 协记 제사기 208대, 梅园路 久丰鼎记 제사기 240대, 恒丰路 源和 제사기 480대, 鼎记 제사기 184대, 光复路 振兴 제사기 240대, 仁锡 제사기 274대, 长安路 瑞丰余福昌泰 (즉 同昌泰) 제사기 480대, 成泰 제사기 432대 등 총 15개 공장이 휴업했다.

당정 협의: 시 사회국은 제사 공장 노동자 파업이 지방 안정에 영향을 미치고 사전에 허가를 받지 않았으므로 확대를 막고 신속하게 해결하기 위해 직원을 파견하여 시 당부와 함께 진상을 조사했다. 현재 조사를 마쳤으므로 어제 오후 1시에 제3과 조정주임 王先青과 시 당부 민훈과 주임 汪曼云을 파견하여 대책을 협의하고 처리 단계를 결정했다.

소환 통지: 시 사회국은 어제 제4구 견사업 공회 및 제사 공장 업계 동업 공회에 통지했다. 통지 사항은 虹口 제사 공장 노동자 파업 건에 대해 본국이 7월 1일 오후 1시에 소환 조사를 실시할 예정이니 사전에 통지하여 귀회가 책임 대표 2명을 파견하여 본국에 와서 소환 조사를 받으십시오. 이에 통지합니다. 중화민국 21년 6월 30일, 국장 吴 亚.

공회 표시: 新声社 기자는 어제 제사 공회 공회 주석 沈 臣氏를 방문했다. 그는 제사 공장 노동자들이 임금을 요구하며 파업을 했다고 말했다. 본회는 신중을 기하기 위해 회원 대회를 개최하여 이 문제를 논의했으나 회원들의 의견은 이번 파업이 공회의 진정한 의사가 아니라 제3자가 배후에서 선동한 것이라고 생각했다. 제사 공장이 이 현상 유지에 勉强 开工 이유는 노동자의 생계를 유지하기 위한 것인데 노동자들이 이해하지 못하고 임금을 인상하려 한다. 쌍방이 서로 유지하기를 희망한다면 임금 인상은 사실상 만에 하나도 불가능하다. 당정 기관이 파업을 선동한 자를 조사하고 노동자에게 복귀를 권유하기를 바란다.

국약업 동업 공회 긴급 회원 총회 소집 166

본월 5일 국약업 동업 공회는 어제 제2차 집행위원회 회의 결의에 따라 7월 5일에 긴급 회원 총회를 소집하여 공회가 제출한 4가지 요구에 대한 답변을 논의하고, 동시에 임기 만료 위원을 개선하기로 결정했다. 모든 총회 소집 통고는 이미 발송되었다. 또한 본회 다수 회원은 이번 파업을 매우 중시하여 동업 공회에 대처 방안을 제안하고 있다. 이에 본회는 최근 접수한 제안을 정리하여 회원 총회에 제출하여 통과 후 실행할 예정이다.

총회 통고: 통고 사항은 본업 공회가 최근 자본가가 조건을 파괴하고 외부 대체 노동자를 거부한다는 구실로 총회를 소집하여 파업을 선동하고, 연일 보도되는 바에 따르면 형세가 매우 심각하다. 본회는 동업자의 위탁을 받아 합법적인 대처와 경과를 처리했으니 명감하시기를 바란다. 이번에는 공회 측에서 지난달 28일에 대표를 파견하여 본회에 와서 구두로 4가지 요구를 제기했다. 상술한 구실 사항 외에 매달 1인당 급여 10원 인상 및 실업자 안치 2가지 요구가 있었다. 당시 본회 상무위원 张梅庵 동지가 중대한 문제이므로 집행위원회에 회부하여 논의한 후 답변하겠다고 답했다. 본 집행위원회는 이번 공회가 제기한 요구가 실질적으로 동업자의 이해관계에 매우 중대한 관계가 있다고 생각하여 동인들이 직권에 제한되어 함부로 모든 것을 결정할 수 없으므로 이번 달 5일 오후 1시에 본 회의실에서 긴급 회원 총회를 소집하여 공회의 요구 사항에 대한 답변을 논의하고, 동시에 규정에 따라 본회 임기 만료 위원을 개선하여 당정 기관에 보고하고 직원을 파견하여 지도하는 것 외에 각 회원에게 회람하여 출석하도록 통지한다. 동업자의 절신한 이해관계에 관한 일이니 각 회원이 정시에 출석해 주시기 바라며, 무한히 간절히 바랍니다. 이에 통지합니다.

회원 제안: 启者 이번 파업 건에 대해 견문이 미치는 바에 따라 약간의 초고를 작성하여 동업 당국 제공에게 참고 자료로 제공하고자 한다. (1) "대체 노동자 문제" 조사한 바에 따르면 이 안건은 본래 화의당 동업자가 공회와 조건이 정해지기 전에 서명한 선결 화약이다. 현재 이미 市社会局 본년 5월 14일 1911호 비령 및 中训部 등 정령이 있으므로 당연히 거절을 주장하고, 그 위법 행위를 확인해야 한다. 그러므로 공회가 계속 강요한다면 동업자는 끝까지 반항해야 하고, 어떠한 희생도 감수해야 한다. (2) "급여 인상 문제" 조사한 바에 따르면 본 문제는 공회가 강력하여 업주 점원에게 이기적인 이중 최면제를 씌우고, 무지한 군중을 유혹하는 전기 없는 원동력이다. 양관하하의 독랄한 수단을 운용하는 것은 조건을 파괴하는 명확한 예증이다. 대처 방법은 다음과 같다. (갑) 사실상 시황이 쇠퇴하고 영업이 부진하여 원래 지출도 유지하기 어렵다고 느끼므로 이번 예상치 못한 수요를 다시 부담하기는 어렵다. 즉, 분문을 증가해도 감당할 수 없다. (을) 인정을 베풀어 원래 급여에 따라 생활을 유지하는 데 충분하다. 옛날식 각 업종 상점과 비교해 보면 이미 우월함을 느낀다. 이번 무리한 수요는 사회의 공평한 평가에 맡기면 이미 불법이다. 나아가 인류의 욕망은 본래 끝이 없다. 이 불경기의 현상에서 자본가는 빚을 내서도 이 무궁한 골짜기를 메울 수 없다. (병) 법률상 강요 수요가 있어도 업주는 지급할 의무가 없다. 바꾸어 말하면 伙方은 요구할 권리가 없다. 법에 따라 단호하게 거절할 수 있다. (3) "안치 문제" 본 문제는 이미 한두 번이 아니다. 공회는 실업 공우를 이용하여 사회 질서 및 공공 안녕을 어지럽히는 것을 목적으로 한다. 그러므로 해결하는 방법도 당연히 법률에 근거해야 한다. (갑) 과거 사실에 근거하여 인용하고 힘껏 주장한다. (을) 법률상 안치 운운은 완전히 한 점포의 행정권을 파괴하는 것이다. 상점과 점伙의 관계는 민법 채편 제2장 제7절 고용 조문 내에서 시작된다. 만약 공회가 자유롭게 지배할 수 있다고 한다면 민법과 명백히 상충된다. 그 기세는 정부 기관이든 인민이든 영리 또는 자선을 목적으로 하는 조합이든 실업자가 있다면 모두 공회의 불법 세력을 빌려 자유롭게 모든 것을 지배할 수 있게 된다. 묻건대 정부는 여전히 정부가 되고 사회는 여전히 사회가 될 수 있는가? 법률의 장엄함은 어디에 있는가? 그러므로 이 불법 안치를 실현하려면 반드시 먼저 현재 적용되는 민법을 폐지해야 한다. 그러므로 본 동업자는 이 민법이 폐지되기 전에는 반드시 이 법에 근거하여 억지로 따르거나 모욕을 참고 완전함을 구해서는 안 된다. (병) 사실상 젊은이의 실업 공우는 대부분 열등 분자이다. 우승 열패, 달윈 진화론에서 자세히 말한다. 이는 자연의 이치이다. 만약 공회가 도리어 거꾸로 행하고 자유롭게 지배한다면 장래의 은환은 감당할 수 없을 것이다. 그러므로 죽음을 맹세하고 반대해야 한다. (정) 법률 부분에 관해서 만약 공회가 월궤 행동 및 불법 행위를 한다면 사법 기관에 소송하여 응당한 죄로 다스릴 수 있다. (4) "조건 문제" 민 16년 본업에서 정한 노자 조건은 그 계약 조문이 대부분 현행 법령과 저촉되므로 본회에서 조건 연구위원회를 조직하여 연구 결과를 준비하고 당국에서 쌍방 수정을 소집할 때 합법 자료를 제공하는 것이 가장 좋다. 조건을 법률과 저촉되는 것으로 약간 열거하면 다음과 같다. (갑) 조건 제1조는 노자 쟁의 중요 사항 처리 극준 조문 제4조와 위배된다. (을) 조건 제2조는 위와 동일한 제5조와 위배되고, 또 공회법 제20조 제3항과 상충된다. (병) 노측의 급여 인상 요구는 물가 지수를 근거로 해야 한다. (참조 위와 동일한 조문 제13조) (정) 내외마당 획분 문제는 상회 시행 세칙 제10조 및 제89 각 조를 참조할 수 있다. 그 제10조에 이르기를 "전 두 조에서 말하는 상업 사용인은 경영 동료 및 직접 영업소에서 노동하는 자에 한한다"라고 되어 있다. 이는 본업 쌍방이 서로 다투는 내외마당의 초점이 다툼이 없는 것이다.

만주리 관원 쫓겨났다고 전보 167

路透社 30일 상해 소식에 따르면 만주리 세관 사무를 관리하는 사람이 보고를 보내어 하얼빈과 통신할 수 없다고 한다. 그의 사무실은 이미 일본 경찰에 포위되어 점거되었고, 세관 직원은 즉시 이사해야 했다고 한다.

미국 영사관에서 정기적으로 중외 내빈 접대 168

미국 병사 오늘 菲岛로 출발 169

일본 사령 좌근 사령이 요즘 상해에 170
