Science

Manufacturing Method of Bleaching Powder (Part 1) 247

— Yunli

To bleach silk, wool, cotton, linen, paper, and other materials, bleaching agents such as chlorine, potassium dichromate, sodium percarbonate, percarbonate, potassium permanganate, and bleaching powder are used. Among these bleaching agents, the most common is bleaching powder. Bleaching powder not only has the function of bleaching but also has the effect of sterilization, so it is very beneficial to mankind. I am now going to introduce the method of manufacturing bleaching powder:

(1) Raw Materials: The raw materials for bleaching powder are chlorine gas and lime. To manufacture bleaching powder, one must first prepare chlorine gas and lime.

(A) Chlorine Gas Manufacturing Method: Put four parts hydrochloric acid and one part manganese dioxide into a flask. Seal the flask tightly with a cork with a hole. Then, use a curved glass tube or rubber tube, insert one end into the hole of the cork, and prepare the other end to be inserted into the hole in the upper or lower part of the bleaching powder box. After preparing in this way, place the flask on a tripod, next to the wooden box, and when manufacturing bleaching powder, use an alcohol lamp to heat under the flask, and chlorine gas will flow into the box through the glass tube.

(B) Lime Selection Method: The quality of the lime is greatly related to the finished product of bleaching powder. When manufacturing, it is advisable to choose thoroughly burned lime chunks, especially newly burned lime, and it is absolutely impossible to use loose lime that has been exposed to the air for a long time. Because loose lime has already absorbed moisture, it cannot absorb a large amount of chlorine gas. After selecting the lime, it is advisable to sprinkle clear water to make it moist and cracked, becoming powder. If there are hard, unburned chunks, they must be screened out with a sieve. But pay attention: the water should not be sprinkled too wet or unevenly. If it is too wet, it will become lime milk and cannot be used. If it is uneven, the ability to absorb chlorine gas will be weak when manufacturing bleaching powder.

(2) Arrangement Method of Manufacturing Box: To manufacture bleaching powder, a wooden box about one foot five inches long and about two feet seven inches high can be used. The inside of the box is lined with lead to prevent corrosion. The middle of the box is separated into six or seven layers with wooden boards, and the distance between each layer is about four inches. However, these wooden boards should be installed so that they can be moved, so that lime can be put in or taken out. Three or four inch square small glass windows should be opened at both ends of the box, so that the shape of the chlorine gas entering the box and combining with the lime can be observed. A small hole should be opened at the upper and lower parts of the box, for introducing chlorine gas. But when the glass tube is inserted into the upper hole, the lower hole should be tightly closed. If the glass tube is replaced and inserted into the lower hole, the upper hole should be tightly closed. After preparing in this way, it is considered successful.

Inexplicable

Such Amateur Performers 248

— Chonglou

If you walk down the street, sometimes you can see various signs hanging at the entrance of a house or alley, such as XX Opera House or XX Society. At night, you can hear the sound of gongs, drums, and fiddles coming from these houses with hanging signs. If you are drawn by curiosity and go inside to visit, you can see that these houses are full of people, sitting, standing, with all kinds of people. These people range from foreign firm employees to courtesans, and everything in between. In addition, you can also see several strangely dressed drama teachers and several slick music masters who play the fiddle and drums.

"Old Wang, sing a song!" So, the one called Old Wang takes a sip of tea, moistens his throat, tells the fiddler to start playing, and then there is a burst of "The shopkeeper has brought over the yellow horse..." After singing a section, he undoubtedly sings very proudly, but he usually has to be humble for a few words, and the others are also complimenting him as usual, although in the hearts of these famous people are filled with many: "Your singing of selling horses is neither the Tan style nor the Yu style," "You shouldn't have dropped the beat on the middle eye in the second sentence," "You should have taken a breath when singing that long phrase," and other dissatisfaction and contempt.

If you inspect those houses, in the beautiful frames hanging on the wall, you can see the charter of their group organization, with the purpose item prominently written: "Our society aims to study art and connect feelings." At that time, you can't help but have doubts in your mind, "What kind of art is this studying? What kind of feelings are they connecting?"

If you are unwilling to be nosy, stay longer, and make further investigations, then leave that place. When you walk out of those noisy and dusty houses, you can take a big breath of fresh air outside.

I myself have also been in and out of opera houses, and I myself have also been called an amateur performer, but what benefits do these opera houses and amateur performers have for society and life? Even I myself am inexplicable!

Sexual Problems

The Landlady's Melancholy 249

— Moyi

The garret has been empty for more than a month; today, a young man who looks like a seventeen or eighteen-year-old student rented it for a monthly rent of six dollars. The landlady stood in the yard, squinting at the young man directing the rickshaw puller to move his simple furniture and luggage. She felt that the young man reflected in her eyes was the same as the lovely young man in her dream last night. Her husband, who was twelve years older than her, worked on a ship and only came back three or four days a month. Only twenty-one years old, she often watched the young couples in the neighborhood during the day, and her heart often stirred up waves of jealousy; at night, she slept alone in bed, and her whole body was often attacked by an inexplicable feeling of depression, and the laughter of the young couples coming from next door was even more embarrassing for her, thinking that they were giving her great humiliation. So, she took one of the young men in the neighborhood as the object of her pursuit of happiness, and fantasized about rosy dreams; in her dreams, she got sweet kisses, hugs, loving jokes, and carnal revelry. Today, a young man suddenly moved into her house, and she thought it was a gift from God. This seventeen or eighteen-year-old young man, she thought, was a child - a child who had not been baptized by love, as long as she let him taste a little bit of love, she could get the enjoyment of youth. She was thinking wildly, when she suddenly heard the young man say to her in a low voice:

"The things are moved in. Should the gate be closed?" "Oh... oh... oh..." She didn't know what she was saying in her mouth, and her face was burning hot. She calmed down and gave him a very charming smile, her face flushed, and slowly walked over to close the gate. She involuntarily followed him to the garret.

She chatted with him in his room for a while; she knew that he was studying in a middle school not far from her house. Because the dormitory in the school was already full of people, he lived outside the school; but as soon as the new dormitory being built was completed, he would move in. She hoped that this new dormitory would be completed after she and he were already immersed in the river of love, and that at that time, he would not have the heart to move away from her arms.

In the morning, she gave him water to wash his face and tidied up his bedding. In the afternoon, when he came back, she specially made a few dishes for him with her own hands and kept him to eat dinner together. She chatted with him, pulling this way and that, and was surprised that she always had so much to say. Sometimes, she gave him a few hints; these hints included all her hopes and passionate love for him. And he seemed to be a fool, not showing anything at all, and seeming not to feel her hints. He lowered his head and blushed, feeling his pulse beating very hard, pressed by her several blatant expressions of love and strong temptations of the opposite sex. Looking at him like this, although she felt very disappointed, she understood that he was still a shy child, and his childlike heart had not been shot by Cupid's arrow. However, for some reason, she couldn't sleep even more at night, and even had no sweet dreams, and her heart was only filled with unbearable melancholy.

He spent more than twenty days in such an atmosphere full of stimulation of the opposite sex. Sometimes he really felt suffocated; but sometimes he thought that the sweet dew of love was irrigating his heart, and perhaps one day it would grow out the tender shoots of love. One day, when he came back in the afternoon, he didn't see her at the door, who welcomed him every day. He was surprised. He entered the door, but there was no sign of her in the yard or in his own room. He put down his books and had just sat down on the chair when she came in. She said in a low voice with a smile:

"Two relatives came from the countryside today. How annoying. They're going to stay here for more than ten days!" After saying that, she smiled and left.

Since her relatives came, he rarely spoke to her; he had to tidy up his bedding himself; and she didn't eat with him anymore. On the contrary, he felt that without her nagging beside him, his life was much quieter. On the fourth day, he said to her apologetically:

"The school's new dormitory has been completed. I'm going to move in."

She stood beside her relatives, her eyes wide with disappointment, a melancholy smile on her face, watching him direct the rickshaw puller to move his simple furniture and luggage away.

Nonsense

The Art of Speaking 250

— Yiyi Guan Master

The day before yesterday, after dinner, my mother jokingly asked a country woman who had just come out and had not been baptized in society, "Do you know how old I am this year?" The woman replied, "I see that madam is at least in her sixties." When we heard it, we couldn't help but burst into laughter, and my mother laughed as well. Because we thought that the woman was really honest and funny. In fact, my mother is not yet sixty years old. Of course, others would say, "Madam is young." But she said, "Madam is at least in her sixties." How could it not be funny? In fact, perhaps she had another kind of psychology, thinking that being old is a blessing and she did not say anything wrong; however, how would she know that she would instead earn us a burst of laughter, making her inexplicable?

Therefore, I feel that the psychology of not wanting to be old is the most common. Often, some people are indeed old, but they insist that others say they are young, especially women, most of whom have this psychology. But there are some people who want to act old and be old-fashioned. Even though they are not yet fifty years old, they insist that others say they are old, and even call themselves "old man" or "old woman." If someone says "young," they will be unhappy. Then, the reason why the woman said that my mother was more than sixty years old may be an expression of this psychology. However, people's psychologies are different. What she thought was correct, others thought was incorrect and funny. From this small and unimportant matter, I have come to realize that when it comes to speaking, one must also have art, especially in modern society, otherwise one cannot cater to people's psychologies and is just a "fool"!

Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court 251

Civil Ruling: In the case of Quan Jia and Hanamu Sheng suing for repayment of debts, the appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the cost of the second instance litigation. ▲ In the case of Li Maochen and Lu Zhangfu appealing for the payment of a loan, the appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the cost of the third instance litigation. ▲ In the case of Risheng and others suing Ti Baike for rent arrears and vacating the house, the appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the cost of the third instance litigation. (June 30)

Shanghai First Special District Local Court 252

Criminal First Instance Judgments

▲ Regarding the case of recidivist robber Li Daqiang, originally handled by the Shanghai Public Concession Mixed Court, Li Daqiang was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for armed robbery with accomplices. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is finalized will be counted towards the execution of the sentence.

▲ Regarding the case of recidivist robber Li Changqi, originally handled by the Shanghai Public Concession Mixed Court, Li Changqi was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for each of the two counts of armed robbery with accomplices, and seven years of imprisonment for one count of robbery with accomplices, totaling twelve years of imprisonment. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is finalized will be counted towards the execution of the sentence.

▲ Regarding the case of robbers Chen Lianyu and others, originally handled by the Shanghai Public Concession Mixed Court, Chen Lianyu, Tian Changfu, and Xu Xiaolianzi were each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for each of the two counts of armed robbery with accomplices, totaling ten years of imprisonment. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is finalized will be counted towards the execution of the sentence.

▲ Regarding the case of recidivist robber Zhao Zhengfu, originally handled by the Shanghai Public Concession Mixed Court, Zhao Zhengfu was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for each of the two counts of armed robbery with accomplices, totaling ten years of imprisonment. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is finalized will be counted towards the execution of the sentence.

▲ In the case of Yu Xixiu Ying suing Yu Genfa and others for offenses against public morals and abandonment, Yu Genfa was found not guilty. The attached civil suit is transferred to the civil court for adjudication.

▲ Huang Faxiang sues Chen Tongsheng for encroachment. Chen Tongsheng is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for appropriating another's property. Chen Tongsheng should return the bicycle to Huang Faxiang and compensate him with $60. The remaining parts of the plaintiff's attached civil suit are rejected.

▲ Gu Qiaoxian versus Moriizumi for assault. The private prosecution is rejected.

▲ Fu Zidong sues Shen Shihua for breach of contract. This case is not accepted.

▲ Strobelena sues Hook Jack for embezzlement. This case is not accepted.

▲ Wang Liangcai is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for habitual theft as a repeat offender.

▲ The Old Gate Police Station sues Zhou Qin and others for possessing firearms and ammunition without permission. Du Yuwei is fined 100 yuan for possessing military handgun bullets without permission.

▲ Yang Hongsheng, a repeat offender for robbery, is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment.

▲ Ding Shougen sues Rong Jinsheng on suspicion of false accusation and assault. Rong Jinshan is found not guilty.

▲ Li Fubin is sentenced to two months of imprisonment with a two-year suspended sentence for the crime of offering bribes.

▲ The Old Gate Police Station sues Liu Changshan and others for theft. Liu Changshan is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for one count of theft, and 30 days of detention for another count of theft.

▲ Ma Qing'en is sentenced to 30 days of detention for one count of theft.

▲ Ye Jinfu is sentenced to 50 days of detention for one count of theft.

▲ Huang Zisheng is fined 10 yuan for gambling.

▲ Yao Congxin and Wang Yucai are each fined 10 yuan for gambling.

▲ Zhang Rujiu is fined 20 yuan for one count of assault.

▲ Lu Xinsoon is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for one count of fraud.

▲ Zhang Wang is sentenced to 30 days of detention for one count of theft.

▲ Wang Yunan and Wang Jiaming are each fined 20 yuan for each count of possessing opium smoking paraphernalia. Wu Mingren and Zhang Lisheng are found not guilty.

▲ Wang Zonghai is fined 100 yuan for one count of theft.

▲ Yao Asi and Ma Guanda are each given a one-month sentence reduction for the joint consumption of opium. Tian Yang and Yang Zhang are each fined 10 yuan for each count of possessing opium smoking paraphernalia.

▲ Civil First Instance Judgments

▲ Zhou Linsheng versus Zhao Futang and others in debt case. Defendant Zhao Futang shall repay the plaintiff 1,500 yuan, plus interest at a monthly rate of 1% from the date of borrowing until the date of execution, and it is confirmed that the plaintiff has a mortgage right on the three-room western half of the brick house belonging to Hong Si Guan, owner of No. 15, Ti Zi Wei, 13th Tu, 23rd Bao, Shangyi. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The litigation costs are borne by the defendant Zhao Futang.

▲ Yongxin Real Estate Company versus Qu Zheng in housing eviction case. Defendant Qu Zheng shall promptly vacate the house at No. 36 Sijing Road and compensate the plaintiff for rental losses at a rate of 65 taels per month from February of this year until the date of execution. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution regarding the house is granted. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

▲ Zhu Xiangrong versus Chen Yixin, shareholder and manager of China Automobile Materials Company, in a debt case. Defendant Chen Yixin, shareholder and manager of China Automobile Materials Company, shall repay the plaintiff 551.72 yuan. If he is unable to pay, the owner of Wang Yue Ji Coal Shop shall be responsible for paying on his behalf. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant Chen Yixin, shareholder and manager of China Automobile Materials Company.

▲ Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Smis versus Rong Ruichang and others in debt case. Defendant Rong Ruichang shall repay the plaintiff 3,274.98 taels of silver and 424.54 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from January 1 of this year until the date of execution. If Rong Ruichang is unable to pay, Li Genxing, the owner of the Jue Lu Hotel, shall be jointly and severally liable for payment. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. Litigation costs are borne equally by both parties.

▲慎餘洋行, Manager Ke Tuo, versus Da Lun Qian Ji Silk Factory and others in debt case. Defendant Da Lun Qian Ji Silk Factory shall repay the plaintiff 14,613.5 taels of silver, plus interest at an annual rate of 8% from November 1, 1926, until the date of execution. If it is unable to pay, the defendant Chen Shuqian shall pay on its behalf. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant Da Lun Qian Ji Silk Factory. Provisional execution is granted in this case.

▲ Shao Maike versus Ekenstein in compensation case. The application is rejected. The costs of restoring the original state and the costs incurred due to the delay are borne by the defendant.

▲ Xu Jingfu versus Lin Jingde and others in a share capital case. Defendants Lin Jingde and Huang Yi shall jointly liquidate and repay the plaintiff's deposit of 1,247.445 yuan and the remaining share capital of 991.356 yuan. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. Litigation costs are borne jointly by defendants Lin Jingde and Huang Yi for 40%, and by the plaintiff for 60%.

▲ Ningkang Company versus Cheng Xiangzhi in a rent arrears case. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 246.6 yuan in rent. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

▲ Sincere Company, Zheng Zhaobin versus Wei Rende in a rent arrears case. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 342 taels of silver in rent, and it is confirmed that the plaintiff has a lien on the movable property placed by the defendant in the leased premises. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

▲ 　Sheng versus Lin A Gen and others in a debt case. Defendants Lin A Gen and Lin Sheng shall jointly repay the plaintiff 150 yuan. This amount shall be repaid jointly at 15 yuan per month. If they are unable to pay, the defendant Chen Yulin shall pay on their behalf. Litigation costs are borne by the defendants Lin A Gen and Lin Sheng.

▲ Taibai Xing versus Jiang Jingyuan and others in a debt case. The defendants shall jointly repay the plaintiff 500 yuan in principal, plus interest, which shall be calculated until the date of execution. Litigation costs are borne by the defendants.

▲ Xu Tongqi versus Guo Hanxing in a debt case. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,301.5 taels of silver and 715.86 yuan, plus legal late payment interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the date of execution. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

▲ 道而格逹司 versus Xu Genxiang in a loan case. The defendants shall jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. Litigation costs are borne jointly and severally by the defendants.

▲ S.A. Vainio, K. P. Mumm versus Xu Lansheng in a rent arrears and eviction case. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 72 yuan in rent. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant for 3/5 and by the plaintiff for 2/5.

▲ Guangye Real Estate Company, Baik, versus Lu Jikang Hospital, Lu Xiulin, in a rent arrears and eviction case. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,225.5 yuan, vacate the premises, and it is confirmed that the plaintiff has a lien on the items placed by the defendant in the leased premises. Provisional execution is granted in this case regarding the eviction. Litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

▲ Tang Zixiang versus Zhou Hengfu and others in a case regarding the return of the goodwill price. The plaintiff's claim is rejected. Litigation costs are borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Fan Keling versus Xu Weixuan and others in a debt case. Defendant Xu Weixuan shall repay the plaintiff 4,500 taels of silver and 7,000 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 9% from September 8, 1928, until the date of execution. Defendant Chen Yonglin shall deduct the land price earned by Xu Weixuan when repaying his deposit, with Xu Weixuan bearing two-thirds of the costs and Chen Yonglin bearing one-third.

▲ Hu Shanshan requests execution in a alimony case with Hu Lansheng. The application is acknowledged by the court. A subsequent order for case execution will be given.

▲ Machia requests the return of evidence in a debt case with Hua Xilifu. The application is acknowledged by the court. Please bring this notice to the court at 9:00 AM on July 2nd to register and collect the evidence.

▲ Thomas Cross requests assistance in execution and collection of the sealing fee in a debt case with Gao Yongkang. The application is acknowledged by the court. Permission is granted to send a letter to the Shanghai Local Court for assistance in execution. The previously paid sealing fee of 10 yuan must be collected. Please bring this notice to the court at 9:00 AM on July 2nd to register and collect the fee.

▲ Hu Lansheng requests the collection of evidence in a alimony case with Hu Shanshan. Please bring this notice to the court at 9:00 AM on July 2nd to register and collect the evidence.

▲ Si Da Company's Accounting Department requests the retention of the proceeds of the sale in a debt case between Li Yinzhang and Li Hanting. The application is acknowledged by the court. Upon investigation, the execution case between Li Yinzhang and Li Hanting has already been settled and dismissed, and the creditor has applied for the revocation of the seizure, which has also been approved. There is no need to discuss the retention of the proceeds of the sale. Please be informed of this ruling.

▲ Chen Xianglin and others request the issuance of a certificate of estate management after the expiration of the public notice period. The application is acknowledged by the court. Permission is granted for the issuance of a certificate of estate management.

▲ Gu Yuntang requests registration for separation from Gu Rongrong. The application is acknowledged by the court. If your son Gu Rongrong does not engage in proper work and wanders around outside, you can certainly claim that you are not involved in his personal debts. However, the parent-child relationship originates from blood lineage, and there is no legal basis for separation. Even if the head of the family orders family members to separate from the household, it should go through the procedure of filing a lawsuit. There is no need to register the request.

Shanghai Second Special District Court 253

Criminal Judgments: The Police Department vs. Yan Shunfa et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Yan Shunfa, also known as Yan Chengfa, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined 100 yuan for the crime of providing his premises for others to smoke opium with the intent to profit. Gong Yougen, Kang Changchun, and Wang Jinquan are each sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined for the crime of smoking opium. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Kang Changchun and Wang Jinquan are granted a three-year suspended sentence. Two opium pipes, two lamps, one needle, and two trays are confiscated.

▲ Police Department vs. Zhu Tugeng, Manslaughter Case (Main Text): Zhu Tugeng is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for causing death due to negligence in business. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. A two-year suspended sentence is granted. The related civil lawsuit is transferred to the Civil Division of this court for trial.

▲ Police Department vs. Yuan A’fa et al., Gambling Case (Main Text): Yuan A’fa is sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan for helping to operate and gathering people to gamble. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. Lin A’bao is given a reduced sentence of one month of imprisonment for helping to operate and gathering people to gamble. The seized eighteen Huahui lottery tickets, one stamp, two pencils, one silver dollar, nine jiao, eight shuangjiao coins, and two hundred and sixty-five copper coins are confiscated.

▲ Police Department vs. Liu Fuyi, Gambling Case (Main Text): Liu Fuyi is fined 140 yuan for gambling. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. Nine Huahui lottery tickets, two Huahui lottery books, one silver dollar, three shuangjiao coins, ninety-two copper coins, and two books are confiscated.

▲ Police Department vs. Hu Yuweng et al., Fraud Case (Main Text): Hu Yuweng (also known as Hu Xiameng) is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan for using fraudulent means to cause others to hand over their property to him with the intent of illegally possessing it. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff in the related civil lawsuit for 420 yuan. Yao Zhao's is found not guilty.

▲ Police Department vs. Sergei Bakov, Robbery Suspicion Case (Main Text): Sergei Bakov is found not guilty.

▲ Police Department vs. Chen Dabao, Gambling Case (Main Text): Chen Dabao is sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined 20 yuan for gathering people to gamble with the intent to profit. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Gambling money and gambling paraphernalia are confiscated according to regulations.

▲ Police Department vs. Lou Chanua, Gambling Case (Main Text): Lou Chanua is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined 150 yuan for helping others gather people to gamble. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Gambling money and gambling paraphernalia are confiscated according to regulations.

▲ Private Prosecution by He Baozhen vs. Chen Dasheng et al., Assault Case (Main Text): This case is not accepted.

▲ Police Department vs. Xu A’san et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Xu A’san is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to smoke opium substitutes. Wang A’san and Fang Xuchu are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Xu Gensheng is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for being a repeat offender in smoking opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Fang Xuchu is granted a two-year suspended sentence. Four opium pipes are confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department vs. Ge Hongcheng et al., Robbery Case (Main Text): Ge Hongcheng, Chen Jinbiao, and Zhao A’gan are each sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for the crime of robbery by a group of three or more. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲ Police Department vs. Chen Huichuan et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Chen Huichuan is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to smoke opium. Shen Huiming is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Opium paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department vs. Sun Futang et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Sun Futang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to smoke opium. Yang Bingsheng and Fang A’long are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Opium pipes, opium bubbles, silver dollars, and copper coins are confiscated according to the list.

▲ Police Department vs. Dai Weisheng et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Dai Weisheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to smoke opium with the intent to profit. Wang Hanting, Shen Xialin, Shen Lu's, Bu Zicai, Zhao Daqiu, and Yongfa are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. Liu Guisheng is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for being a repeat offender in smoking opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Shen Xialin and Shen Lu's are each granted a two-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated according to the list.

▲ Fei Tingyou vs. Chen Zhiping, Appeal on Fraudulent Acquisition of Property Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected.

▲ Police Department vs. Liang Jie et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Liang Jie is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 400 yuan for the crime of providing his premises for others to smoke opium with the intent to profit. Lu Yunji, Jian Gui, and Liang Ji are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined for the crime of smoking opium. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Li Shun is found not guilty. Opium paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list.

▲ Police Department vs. Ye Zhi, Snatching Case (Main Text): Ye Zhiwen is sentenced to ten months of imprisonment for being a repeat offender in snatching other people's property. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲ Police Department vs. Zhang Yiqi, Opium Case (Main Text): Zhang Yiqi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 600 yuan for selling opium. If the fine is not paid, three yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Opium sales ledger, silver dollars, and copper coins are confiscated.

▲ Police Department vs. Chen Daoyou et al., Theft Case (Main Text): Chen Daoyou is sentenced to forty days of detention for theft. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of detention. Ye Yuchun is fined 20 yuan for knowingly purchasing stolen goods. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be counted as one day for two yuan of the fine.

▲ Police Department vs. Wu Shengmei, Theft Case (Main Text): Wu Shengmei is sentenced to ten days of detention for the crime of theft. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of detention.

▲ Police Department vs. Xu Zisheng, Opium Case (Main Text): Xu Zisheng is fined 30 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be counted as one day for two yuan of the fine. One each of opium pipe, opium lamp, opium needle, opium tongs, opium pick, and opium tray are confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department vs. Wang Gensheng, Gambling Case (Main Text): Wang Gensheng is fined 200 yuan for gambling. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. Huahui lottery tickets and gambling money are confiscated according to the list.

▲ Private Prosecution by Song Yiming vs. Driver No. 376 of the Route 18 Trolley Bus, Negligence Causing Injury and Damage Case (Main Text): This private prosecution is not accepted.

▲ Police Department vs. Zhao Yousan et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Zhao Yousan is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 60 yuan for helping to provide his premises for others to smoke opium with the intent to profit. Xu A’cai is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for being a repeat offender in eating opium. Xu Bingsheng is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Xu Bingsheng is granted a three-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia is confiscated according to the list.

▲ Police Department vs. Ge Guangkai et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Ge Guangkai (also known as Ge A’er) is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for being a repeat offender in providing his premises for others to smoke opium substitutes with the intent to profit. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Hu Yongsheng and Lu Haiquan are granted a three-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia and red pills are confiscated according to the list.

Civil Rulings: Zhang Maozhi, transferee of Huang Chunrong of Qianyi Hotel, petition for registration: The petition is acknowledged. All external debts of the hotel shall still be handled by the petitioner in conjunction with Huang Chunrong, who shall notify all creditors to be present for a clear handover to avoid disputes. This is the ruling.

▲ Yang’s petition for withdrawal of appeal: The petition is acknowledged. Since the case has been settled amicably, the appeal is allowed to be withdrawn. This is the ruling.

▲ Ha Yanqing’s petition for revocation of provisional attachment: The petition is acknowledged. Upon investigation, the original ruling of the Civil Division of this court stated that if the debtor provides the requested amount (448 yuan) as security, a petition may be made to suspend or revoke the provisional attachment. As requested by the petitioner, the above amount of cash must be provided as security in accordance with the ruling before the revocation can be approved. If only a reliable guarantor is found, it does not comply with the original ruling and approval is difficult to grant. This is the ruling.

▲ Zhu Weiruo’s petition for postponement of execution: The petition is acknowledged. Upon investigation, the case has long been finalized. The petitioner is required to pay off the owed deposit of 9,000 taels within one week. The request for postponement of execution is not in accordance with the law and approval is difficult to grant. This is the ruling.

▲ French company Yongxing Foreign Firm's petition for withdrawal of funds: The petition is acknowledged. Upon investigation, the proceeds from the sale of the movable property of the China Navigation Company, which was attached by the former French Concession Court, amount to 285 taels. After reviewing the case file, please come to the court at 9:00 AM on July 1 to collect the funds. This is the ruling.

▲ Zhang Yuzhao's petition for enforcement: The petition is acknowledged. This court previously received a letter from the Shanghai District Court requesting assistance in enforcement. However, the petitioner’s address was not clearly stated, making it impossible to serve the case. It is now stated that a date for convening and enforcement can be arranged. This is the ruling.

▲ Sun, from Jicheng Silver Company, petition for entrustment of assistance in execution by the Shanghai District Court: The petition is acknowledged. A letter shall be sent to the Shanghai District Court requesting assistance in execution, and the petitioner shall file a petition with the court. This is the ruling.

▲ Hejihao’s petition for unsealing: The petition is acknowledged. An official shall be instructed to unseal. This is the ruling.

▲ Slesman's petition for determination of installment payment method: The petition is acknowledged. The case shall be served and a hearing held. This is the ruling.

▲ Ju Feng Real Estate Company, Liang Ruian’s petition for issuance of certificates and objects: The petition is acknowledged. The four house tickets previously submitted are to be collected from the court immediately. This is the ruling.

▲ Zhu Gu's objection to Zhu Xiaoshan's petition for registration: The petition is acknowledged. Since the petitioner has objections to Zhu Xiaoshan's petition for registration, a formal lawsuit should be filed for resolution. This is the ruling.

Civil Judgments: Huafu Paint Store vs. Yihe Store Manager Wang Liangcen, Goods Payment Case: The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 340 taels of silver for the goods. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Yin Yu Company, Wu Huaichun vs. Zheng Jinzhao, Luhao, et al., Rent Arrears Case: The defendants shall each pay the plaintiff 354.20 yuan in rent. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the defendants.

▲ Kaili Foreign Firm vs. Aibudi, Gold Payment Case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 223.75 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the date of final execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Xiyuan Rongji Bathhouse vs. Yiyuan Coal Store, Goods Payment Appeal Case: The appeal is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲ Xin Ruihe Foreign Firm vs. 21 People of Huanqiu Hotel, Xue Yaohua, Rent Arrears Case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 920 taels of silver in rent and provide a reliable guarantor and sign a guarantee agreement. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Huang Chunrong vs. Xue Heshang, Debt Arrears Appeal Case: The original judgment is changed, and the appellee’s claim is rejected. The litigation costs for both the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellee.

▲ Wang Zifang vs. Fuxingju, Shao Enpu, Return of Landlord Case: The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Teng Yongchang vs. Zheng Dehe, Goods Payment Case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,293 taels, 7 qian, and 9 fen of silver, plus 955.84 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Cheng Shutang vs. Fang Xiangsen et al., Debt Arrears Case: Defendant Fang Xiangsen shall repay the plaintiff 675 taels of silver, plus interest at a rate of 1.5% per month from December 15, 1931, until the date of final execution. If the execution is ineffective, Shi Wenbin shall be responsible for clearing the debt. The litigation costs shall be borne by defendant Fang Jusen.

▲ Huizhong Silver Company General Manager Mark vs. Mrs. Sha Aifu et al., Loan Case: Defendant Mrs. Sha Sha Aifu shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the date of final execution. If the execution is ineffective, Sha Sha Aifu shall be responsible for clearing the debt. The litigation costs shall be borne by defendant Mrs. Sha Sha Aifu.

▲ Tonghe Coal Store vs. New York Laundry Company, Goods Payment Case: The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 65.50 yuan for the goods in two installments, with one month as one period. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Civil Rulings: Fan Qingzeng’s petition for withdrawal of funds: The petition is acknowledged. Upon investigation, the debtor has not paid any funds to the court, so no funds can be withdrawn. Regarding the alleged destruction of the seal, an official has been instructed to investigate and take action. In addition, the seal should be quickly re-applied and the property appraised and auctioned. This is the ruling.

▲ Mingxing Film Company’s petition for provisional disposition execution: The petition is acknowledged. The petitioner and Gu Wuwei are involved in a copyright lawsuit, and Gu Wuwei has filed a petition for provisional disposition, which has been ruled on by this court. According to the petitioner’s statement, the Romance of West Chamber film is being screened at the Nanjing Theater, and 2,715 tickets have already been sold today. It is requested that the provisional disposition be temporarily suspended today. Upon investigation of the above, the described situation may cause misunderstandings among the audience and lead to disputes. The petitioner shall immediately provide a guarantee of 5,000 yuan to temporarily suspend the execution today. The screening shall be suspended in accordance with the previous ruling from tomorrow onwards. This is the ruling.

▲ Zhang Shichuan’s petition for registration: The petition is acknowledged. If the matters stated by the petitioner are true, there are appropriate remedies under current laws. The requested registration for prevention is unnecessary. This is the ruling.

▲ Ouyang Chaojin's request for temporary suspension of execution: The petition is acknowledged. This court has set a deadline for payment. The case funds must be paid immediately without any excuses or delays. This is the ruling.

Liu Chenglin's statement to move Buddhist statues: This petition is acknowledged. This is the ruling.

Shanghai Local Court 254

Civil Judgement: Zhuang Yiyuan versus Zhu Ashun et al. for a rent case (Main Text): Defendant Zhu Ashun shall repay the plaintiff thirty-six yuan in rent. Zhu Liancheng shall immediately vacate the house. Of the litigation costs, one-third, corresponding to the withdrawn portion, shall be borne by the plaintiff, and the remaining two-thirds shall be borne by the defendant Zhu Ashun. ▲ Tang Fenglou versus Zhao Wenjie et al. for a rent case (Main Text): Defendant Zhao Wenjie shall settle with the plaintiff fifty yuan and vacate the house. If unable to repay, defendant Ding Genyuan shall be responsible for repayment. One-third of the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Zhao Wenjie. ▲ Ruling regarding Min Xihua et al. versus Min Xixun concerning land in an appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of this trial. Pan Lesan et al. versus the owner of Yuankang & Co. for a goods payment case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff Pan Lesan seven hundred and fifty-two taels of silver for goods, and shall also repay the plaintiff Zhang Linhe two hundred and forty-seven yuan for goods, both with interest calculated at a rate of five percent per annum from the date of the lawsuit until the day of enforcement. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants proportionally. ▲ Zhang Amao versus Yao Jinhua for a debt case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff two thousand yuan in borrowed money, with interest at the agreed rate of one percent and one mill per month from May 31st, 15th year of the Republic, until the day of enforcement. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Monk Qunzhou versus Chen Quan for a mutual lawsuit regarding base land and door access (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The disputed Taiping Gate shall be immediately blocked by the plaintiff and restored to its original condition. The litigation costs for both the lawsuit and counterclaim shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Liu Heshang et al. versus Gong Guoxun et al. for a debate concerning land property execution (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. Ruling regarding Tang Shilin versus Shen Tangyuehe for an appeal concerning the return of objects (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Ruling regarding Dao Yangmo et al. versus Wang Yuchen for a debt case (Main Text): This case shall be transferred to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court for trial. Yuan Youdao versus Yuan Youyi for an appeal concerning inheritance (Main Text): The original judgment is overturned. The house property, belongings, and miscellaneous items left by Yuan Zaiming shall be divided equally between the two parties. Yuan Youdao's appeal is rejected. Yuan Youdao, the appellant, shall bear the litigation costs of both the first and second instances. Zhou Rongsheng versus Gao Haifeng for an appeal concerning eviction (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. Chen Jinshi versus Zhu Jingyong for an appeal concerning a loan (Main Text): The original judgment is overturned. The lawsuit filed by the appellee in the first instance is rejected. The appellee shall bear the litigation costs of both the first and second instances. ▲ Li Weinong et al. versus Jiang Lianquan for an appeal concerning compensation for losses (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Huang Shenglu versus Sun Yongzhang for an objection to land and property execution (Main Text): The disputed land and property are confirmed to be owned by the plaintiff and shall be unsealed and not used for the execution in the debt case of Sun Yongzhang versus Huang Yanhui. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Gu Jiuhe versus Cai Yougui for an appeal concerning old land (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of this trial. Gu Lisheng versus Cai Yougui for an appeal concerning the withdrawal of land (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of this trial. ▲ Qian Zitang versus Ye Shuqin for an appeal concerning rent (Main Text): The original judgment is changed. Appellant Qian Zitang shall, after deducting the eighteen yuan that should be returned, settle with Ye Shuqin for the thirty-six yuan and two fen for overpayment of rent. Appellant Ye Shuqin shall return all rented property and other items to appellant Qian Zitang in full. Appellant Ye Shuqin shall bear the litigation costs of this trial and the first instance lawsuit. Appellant Qian Zitang shall bear the litigation costs of the first instance counterclaim.

Civil Instructions: Yang Dongsheng's request to record the prevention of his daughter-in-law's escape is noted. According to the statement, the man's daughter-in-law previously reported to the police station due to an incident and followed instructions to keep his daughter-in-law under family restraint, which should ensure her obedience and stability. There is no need to worry excessively. If there is any reason for her to escape, it is not something that can be resolved by recording it. The request should not be discussed. This is the instruction.

Criminal Judgement: Zhao Jinbiao's case of false accusation (Main Text): Zhao Jinbiao is acquitted. ▲ Chen Baosheng et al.'s case of obstructing official duties (Main Text): Chen Baosheng is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for obstructing official duties, with two days of detention equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Yu Jinglin is innocent. ▲ Zhang Demao et al.'s opium case (Main Text): Zhang Demao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium, and is also sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. The determined execution is seven months of imprisonment and a fine of seventy yuan. Yang Guifu, Li Changsheng, and Zhang Zhushi are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for smoking opium. If the fines are not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of detention. Two days of detention are equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Three opium pipes, one opium lamp, two qian of opium ash, one opium spoon, and one opium cage are all confiscated. ▲ Zhu Fushan's case of illegally transporting firearms (Main Text): Zhu Fushan is fined one hundred and twenty yuan for illegally transporting military firearms and ammunition without permission. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of detention. One day of detention is equivalent to one yuan of fine. ▲ Sun Xiaogen et al.'s theft case (Main Text): Sun Xiaogen, Yang Longbao, and Wu A'gen are each sentenced to six months of imprisonment for attempted theft committed by a group of three or more people, with two days of detention equivalent to one day of imprisonment. ▲ Wang Dayou et al.'s opium case (Main Text): Wang Dayou is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium with the intention of making profit, and is also sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. The determined execution is seven months of imprisonment and a fine of seventy yuan. If the fines are not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of detention. Two days of detention are equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Wang Haigen is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of detention. Two days of detention are equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Four opium pipes, one opium scale, three opium lamps, one opium tray, three opium bubbles, one opium spoon, one opium box, and four hundred red pills are confiscated and burned. ▲ Ruling regarding He Xiaoyu's complaint against Li Yufeng for false accusation (Main Text): This private prosecution is rejected. ▲ Jin Fusheng's fraud case (Main Text): Jin Fusheng is fined thirty-five yuan for fraud. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of detention. One day of detention is equivalent to one yuan of fine. ▲ Cai Lingzhen's opium case (Main Text): Cai Lingzhen is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for smoking opium, with a two-year suspended sentence. ▲ Gu Guibao's complaint against Zhang Jinxian for fraud (Main Text): This private prosecution is not accepted. ▲ Wang Wencai's theft case (Main Text): Wang Wencai is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for theft committed by a group of three people, and is also sentenced to thirty days of detention for taking possession of property belonging to others, to be executed concurrently. Two days of detention are equivalent to one day of imprisonment. ▲ Meng San's embezzlement case (Main Text): Meng San is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for embezzling property held in the course of business, with two days of detention equivalent to one day of imprisonment. Meng San shall return fifty yuan to Yan Caoshi for collection.

Civil Judgement: Wang Wangshi versus Wang Shunsheng et al. for a compensation case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Shanghai Lihé Foreign Firm versus Baoxing Second Flour Mill for a payment case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Guangyuanchang et al. versus Li Sen et al. for a goods payment case (Main Text): The defendants shall be jointly and severally liable to repay the plaintiff Guangyuanchang three hundred and sixty yuan and two fen for goods, Guangmaotai one thousand seven hundred and twenty-four yuan, eight jiao, eight fen, and seven li for goods, Tongfuhào two thousand and fifty-six yuan, five jiao, and four fen for goods, Yongtaihao one thousand eight hundred and forty-six yuan, two jiao, and two fen for goods, and Tianchenghào one hundred and ninety-one yuan, three jiao, and five fen for goods. The defendants shall be jointly and severally liable for the litigation costs. ▲ Shen Chenggan versus Zhang Daishi for a case of severing relations (Main Text): The family relationship between the plaintiff and the defendant is permitted to be severed. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Xue Huanying versus Ni Lingen for a debt appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Chen Weigu versus Wang Zhizhu for a case of fulfilling a marriage contract (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Yang Xichun versus Song Jialong for a debt appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of this trial. ▲ Shen Hongxun et al. versus Jin Hongchang for a rent appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Pan Guangrong versus Wang Shilian for a bill payment case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff two thousand yuan, with statutory interest calculated at a rate of five percent per annum from June 1st, 20th year of the Republic, until the day of enforcement. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Cao A'gen versus Cao Yuansheng for a debt case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Zhao Yulin versus Jiang Xuehao for a debt case (Main Text): Defendant Jiang Xuehao shall repay the plaintiff three hundred yuan of silver, with a monthly interest rate of one fen and five li from May 17th, 20th year of the Republic, until the day of settlement. The five yuan already paid in interest is permitted to be deducted. If Jiang Xuehao is unable to repay, Hu Yusheng and Jiao Huanzhang shall be jointly and severally liable to repay on his behalf. Defendant Jiang Xuehao shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Ding Cunlin versus Li Mingsheng et al. for a loan case (Main Text): The defendants shall jointly repay the plaintiff one hundred and fifty yuan of silver. Of the litigation costs, one-half corresponding to the withdrawn portion shall be borne by the plaintiff, and the remaining one-half shall be borne by the defendants equally. ▲ Jin Heshang versus Wu Shukang for a compensation appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance. ▲ Lu Xiaomao versus Su Fugen for a breach of contract case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Yu Aqiao versus Liu Yongfu for a rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff two hundred yuan in rent. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Cao Zhenfa versus Zhang San et al. for a hui payment appeal case (Main Text): The original judgment is overturned. Zhang San shall repay appellant Cao Genyan four hundred yuan of hui payments. If unable to repay, Shen Peilin shall be responsible for repayment on his behalf. The appeals of Zhang San and Shen Peilin, as well as the remaining appeals of Cao Genyan, are all rejected. Appellant Zhang San shall bear the litigation costs of both the first and second instances.
